- **#680 fix(onboarding): derive multi-adapter `config/active_sources.txt` from source-selection emission, not just the RapidAPI branch.** Pre-#680 the injector mapped `rapidapi_feed.txt` → `config/active_sources.txt` 1:1, so a candidate who answered "a, b, c" in the Phase-3g source-selection question got an `active_sources.txt` containing only the RapidAPI adapter — the company-feed (`feed-urls.txt`) and Gmail-alerts (`linkedin-alerts.md`) branches captured their own data files but never enabled their adapters, leaving `greenhouse`, `ashby`, `lever`, and `gmail_linkedin` dormant on every fresh stack until the operator manually edited `/settings/active-sources/`. Three coordinated changes in `findajob.onboarding.injector`. (1) New `_derive_active_sources(found)` helper consumes the three emission files and returns the ordered adapter list: the RapidAPI entry from `rapidapi_feed.txt` (first non-comment line), `greenhouse, ashby, lever` when `feed-urls.txt` has at least one real URL, and `gmail_linkedin` when `linkedin-alerts.md` is non-empty. (2) The 1:1 entry `"rapidapi_feed.txt": "config/active_sources.txt"` is removed from `_OPTIONAL_DESTINATIONS`; the derived content is staged as its own tempfile inside the existing transactional `os.replace` loop, preserving the all-or-nothing commit guarantee from #631. (3) The post-write gate-decision loop that routes to `/onboarding/feed-config/` now skips adapters with empty `required_env_vars` — feed-config exists to onboard API keys; `gmail_linkedin` (handled by the downstream Gmail-config gate) and the public-API adapters (`greenhouse`/`ashby`/`lever`) check their configuration differently and would otherwise mis-route to feed-config after the multi-adapter derivation. `_backup_relpaths()` lists `config/active_sources.txt` explicitly so re-finalize recoverability survives the dict-entry removal. Eight unit tests on the helper plus five inject-level integration tests cover all five 3g combinations (a-only / b-only / c-only / a+b+c / "none") and verify both the file content AND its presence/absence — the latter is what `/settings/active-sources/`'s banner-state check at `findajob.web.routes.board._active_sources_banner_state` actually keys on. **No `migration-required`** — onboarding behavior fix, no schema/env/cron changes. Closes #680.

### Migration required

- **#681** — the fix reinterprets `data/.onboarding-complete` present + `config/active_sources.txt` absent as "user picked none in onboarding" (returns `[]`) instead of "fall back to the 7-adapter default". Before bumping to the version containing this fix, audit each stack for this exact cell and, where present, write the default list to `active_sources.txt` so triage continues to fire its previously-implicit adapters. One-liner per stack: `sudo -u <stack-user> bash -c 'if [ -f <stack-state-dir>/data/.onboarding-complete ] && [ ! -f <stack-state-dir>/config/active_sources.txt ]; then printf "# Managed by /settings/active-sources/. Edit there to keep this file in sync.\njobs-api14\njobs-api14-indeed\njsearch\ngreenhouse\nashby\nlever\ngmail\n" > <stack-state-dir>/config/active_sources.txt; fi'`. As of the verification done on 2026-05-15 only **alice** is in this cell (sentinel from Apr 24 under legacy onboarding, never wrote the file); operator's own stack, papa, judy, clean, and staging already have an explicit `active_sources.txt`; dave and tango have neither sentinel nor file so they take the default path unchanged. Stacks that have completed onboarding *after* this fix lands and intentionally picked "none" must NOT receive this seed.

## [0.25.0] — 2026-05-15

### Fixed
- **#666 fix(interview_prep): raise `max_tokens` to 16384 + surface `finish_reason="length"` via new `openrouter_truncated` log event.** Pre-#666 the interview_prep role config carried `max_tokens: 4096` against `openrouter:anthropic/claude-opus-4.7` (a reasoning model). Reasoning models burn output tokens on reasoning before emitting content, so the cap silently truncated the artifact — `interview_prep_complete` events showed `chars=14000+` in late April, dropping to `chars=11906/12024/12336` by 2026-05-11 onward, with one catastrophic `chars=682` case (Amazon AWS, 2026-05-14 13:19 PT) where the model burned essentially the entire 4096-token budget on reasoning before content. Two coordinated changes. (1) **`config/roles/interview_prep.md` `max_tokens: 4096` → `16384`** — matches the same fix shape as #639 (fit_analyst) and #632 (onboarding voice-samples), both also reasoning-model output-budget exhaustion. Opus 4.7 supports far higher output ceilings than 16384, so the bump is well within model limits; typical content is ~4k tokens, so the new ceiling is ~4× headroom. (2) **Diagnostic enhancement in `findajob.llm.role_runner.run_role`** — when `result.finish_reason == "length"`, log a structured `openrouter_truncated` event to `pipeline.jsonl` carrying `role`, `job_id`, `completion_tokens`, and `content_chars`. Pre-#666 `run_role()` returned the partial string with no surfaced signal of truncation; the caller's only check was `len(output_md) < 500`, which lets every >500-char truncation through as "complete". The new diagnostic benefits *every* role that calls run_role (prep flow's briefing/resume/cover, scoring, fit_analyst) — future max_tokens exhaustion becomes immediately greppable in pipeline.jsonl instead of felt as quality drift. 3 new tests in `test_role_runner_truncation_log.py` cover the three finish_reason cases — `"length"` fires the event, `"stop"` does not, and `None` (backwards compat) does not. `_run_interview_prep`'s existing `len(output_md) < 500` guard is unchanged — it remains the catastrophic-failure check; the new event is the diagnostic for the silent-truncation case. **No `migration-required`** — config frontmatter edit + role_runner observability addition; no schema/env/cron changes. Closes the truncation half of #666; the parity half (Edit + Copy-MD buttons on Interview Prep) shipped earlier in this Unreleased window.
- **#606 fix(web): dashboard burn-rate widget — local-tz week anchor + prep/scoring split.** Pre-#606 the widget at `templates/_cost_widget.html` could read "This week $0.00" on Saturday evenings despite plenty of LLM activity in `cost_log`. Two compounding causes — `weekly_spend()` anchored weeks at UTC Sunday 00:00 (= PT Sat 17:00 PDT / 16:00 PST), and the helper excluded `operation='score'` so during low-prep stretches the prep-only total read $0.00 even while daily scoring spent tens of dollars. Two coordinated changes. (1) **Local-tz week anchor.** `weekly_spend(conn, weeks=4, tz="UTC")` now takes an IANA tz parameter; boundaries are Sunday 00:00 in that tz, computed in Python via `zoneinfo` then converted to UTC for the SQL filter, so DST transitions resolve correctly per-anchor. `landing.py` reads `os.environ.get("TZ", "UTC")` and passes it through — every container already sets `TZ` per stack (`America/Los_Angeles` on operator's, `America/New_York` on alice's, etc.), so the widget anchor follows the operator's perceived "this week" without new config. (2) **Prep/scoring split.** `WeekRow` becomes `(week_start, prep_usd, scoring_usd)` and `projected_monthly()` returns a `ProjectedMonthly` dataclass with `prep_usd` and `scoring_usd` fields (each `float | None`). The widget renders four rows — "This week — prep", "This week — scoring", "Projected month — prep", "Projected month — scoring" — and a footnote citing the active tz: *"Week anchored at Sunday 00:00 {tz}. Sourced from `cost_log.cost_usd`."* Tests in `test_cost_rollups.py` cover the tz boundary, the prep/scoring split for both `weekly_spend` and `projected_monthly`, and the rendered widget (`test_landing_renders_cost_widget_with_prep_and_scoring`); the existing `_insert_cost_log` test helper switches from Sunday-anchored to exact `-N×7 days` offsets so it's no longer flaky when CI runs at UTC times where UTC Sunday and PT Sunday differ. No schema change, no migration. Closes #606.
- **#658 fix(rejection_detector): widen IMAP `rejection_sender_allowlist` to parity with classifier `SENDER_FINGERPRINTS`.** Pre-#658 the IMAP allowlist was a strict subset of the classifier's known platforms — IMAP carried 4 full-address entries (`no-reply@us.greenhouse-mail.io`, `…@eu.greenhouse-mail.io`, `…@ashbyhq.com`, `…@hire.lever.co`), the classifier knew 8 (those 4 plus `myworkday.com`, `smartrecruiters.com`, `email.careers.microsoft.com`, `oracle.com`). The IMAP `FROM` filter silently dropped every Workday / SmartRecruiters / Microsoft / Oracle rejection before the classifier could see it; surfaced by #642 (`cyrusone@myworkday.com` rejection logged `count: 0` across every scan cycle in the window). Three coordinated changes. (1) **Bare-domain entries.** `DEFAULT_REJECTION_ALLOWLIST` switches from full email addresses to bare domains and grows to 8 entries — RFC 3501 `SEARCH FROM` is substring-match, so `FROM "myworkday.com"` matches `cyrusone@myworkday.com` without enumerating per-tenant local-parts. Validated against operator's mailbox: bare-domain returns identical UID counts to the full-address form for the 3 already-allowlisted platforms, and surfaces 14 historical rejection-shaped messages currently invisible (6 Workday, 4 Microsoft, 4 Oracle, 0 SmartRecruiters in a 30-day window). (2) **Union-on-load (`load_config`).** Treats `DEFAULT_REJECTION_ALLOWLIST` as a floor: returns `list(DEFAULT) + [persisted entries not in DEFAULT]`. Existing tester stacks pick up new senders on the next pipeline cycle without a schema bump or a config-edit prompt. Operator customizations (entries not in DEFAULT) survive verbatim. Validator widened to accept bare-domain entries (non-empty string, no spaces, contains `.`). (3) **Round-trip regression test** (`test_workday_rejection_round_trip_through_fetcher_to_classifier`) drives the real `fetch_new_messages_for_rejection_scan` codepath against a Workday-shape fixture, asserts the message survives the IMAP layer, then asserts the classifier outputs `confidence='high'`. Closes the "test real codepath when extracting" gap for this surface. New fixtures: `tests/fixtures/rejection_emails/{smartrecruiters,microsoft,oracle}/rejection.eml`. Workday tenants on custom mail domains (`talent.{company}.com` instead of `myworkday.com`) still slip the IMAP layer; tracked separately as #659 (broader-pattern Option B/C from #658's body). Closes #658; followup to #642's diagnosis.
- **#623 fix(onboarding): clear `error_state` on successful turn/start + OOB-empty the in-page banner slot.** A credit-exhaustion error during the onboarding interview correctly surfaced to the user as a banner, but the banner persisted across recovery even after the user topped up their account and the interview resumed successfully — confusing because the system had self-corrected. Two compounding causes — `set_error()` wrote `session.error_state` to SQLite but nothing cleared it on subsequent success (every `/resume` re-rendered the banner from the DB row), and `templates/onboarding/interview.html`'s banner div had no `id` so the success-turn HTMX partial couldn't target it. Fix: new `clear_error()` in `session_store` called in both `/turn` and `/start` success branches (`/start` was the advisor-caught second case — a failed first attempt persists `error_state` on the credentials-only row, the retried `/start` succeeds but `/resume` still surfaces the banner; same bug class, same fix); banner div now carries `id="error-banner"` and success-turn HTMX response includes an OOB-swap that empties it. Regression tests cover both the recovery transition and the `/start` retry case. **No `migration-required`** — pure web/onboarding behavior fix. Closes #623.
- **#625 fix(ops): warn at container startup when data dir lives on a non-native filesystem (macOS / Windows Docker Desktop unsupported).** External user reported `SQLITE_CORRUPT` mid-batch in `triage.py` on macOS Docker Desktop; no corruption observed on supported Linux-on-Linux platforms. Decision recorded in #664 PR: macOS / Windows Docker Desktop is unsupported (gRPC-FUSE / VirtioFS / 9p / drvfs have known SQLite-WAL incompatibilities). Two coordinated changes: (1) `ops/entrypoint.sh` step 2.5 runs `stat -f -c %T` on `$JSP_BASE/data` and emits a stderr warning when the FS type matches `fuseblk` / `fuse.*` / `virtiofs` / `9p` / `drvfs`. Warning, not abort — corruption is observed in practice but not guaranteed on first boot, and a refusal to start is worse than the eventual recoverable failure. (2) `docs/getting-started/install-docker.md` adds a "Supported platforms" section near the top; existing macOS mention in §1 reworded to point at the supported-platforms note. **No `migration-required`** — purely additive observability + docs. Closes #625 (PR #664).
- **#656 fix(fetch_jd): autofix degenerate gmail_linkedin titles from LinkedIn API response.** Self-emailed LinkedIn URLs from the Android share-flow landed in `jobs.title` as the bare URL string (e.g. `https://www.linkedin.com/jobs/view/4341101773/`); the iOS variant on the same flow can store the company name. `fetch_linkedin_job_data` already paid for an API response carrying the real title, but only surfaced `description` and `company` — the title field was silently discarded. Three coordinated changes: (1) **fetcher** — `fetch_linkedin_job_data` now extracts `payload["title"]` (via `clean_title()`) and returns it alongside the existing fields, with sentinel `title=None` on all error/empty paths. (2) **fetcher cache** — `fetch_jd`, on the `gmail_linkedin` branch, populates `job["_linkedin_title"]` from the API result, mirroring the existing `_linkedin_company` cache. (3) **triage** — new degeneracy predicate `findajob.cleaning.is_degenerate_title(title, company, url)` flags titles that start with `http(s)://`, equal the URL, equal the company string, are shorter than 6 characters, or match the bare-numeric job-ID pattern (`\d{5,}`). The triage orchestrator's main loop, immediately after the existing company-resolution block, swaps in `_linkedin_title` when the stored title is degenerate, recomputes `fingerprint`/`loose_fingerprint`, and re-checks for collisions against rows that already carry the real title (mirrors the company-resolution dedupe path). A new `linkedin_title_autofix` pipeline.jsonl event records each in-flight autofix; collisions emit `dupe_after_title_resolution`. **Backfill:** `scripts/backfill_linkedin_titles.py` (with `--dry-run` and `--limit N` flags) walks pre-existing `gmail_linkedin` rows whose stored title is degenerate, re-fetches via the same `fetch_linkedin_job_data` path, applies the swap, and writes one `audit_log` row per update keyed `'title'`. No new API spend — every LinkedIn API response triage already pays for now surfaces a usable title field. Closes #656; followup to #645's investigation.

### Added
- **#666 feat(web): Interview Prep parity with #210 — Edit + Copy-MD buttons on `* Interview Prep - *` artifacts.** Pre-#666 the Interview Prep `.md` (written by `findajob.interview.orchestrator` on POST `/board/jobs/{fp}/interview`) classified to the `Other` bucket in `_classify_file()` and rendered without the ✎ Edit button or the 📋 Copy MD button — every other generated material got both via #210 and #347, but interview prep was deliberately out of #210's allowlist. Surfaced via in-app feedback widget on 2026-05-14. Single classifier extension at `src/findajob/web/routes/materials.py`: new `_GROUP_RULES` tuple `(" Interview Prep - ", "Interview Prep", 9)` (sort order 9 places it at the tail of the per-folder view — interview prep is the last artifact generated, only after the user advances to the Interviewing stage), new `_GROUP_DESCRIPTIONS` entry in the "For your eyes only." voice (`"Interview notes for {title} at {company} — STAR stories, questions to ask, tough Qs to anticipate. Read before each round to anchor your talking points. For your eyes only."`), and new `_FILE_HINTS` entries for the `.md` and `.docx` pair. The rest of #210's machinery is filename-pattern-agnostic: the POST `/materials/{fp}/files/{name}` route gates on `_classify_file() != "Other"`, the template's Edit button on `g.label != 'Other'`, the Copy-MD button on `f.ext == 'md'` only, the `.docx` auto-regen on `docx_path.is_file()` (Interview Prep always produces a `.md`+`.docx` pair via `orchestrator.py:221` using the same `strip-bookmarks.lua` + `reference.docx` pandoc flags that `render_md_to_docx` uses, so auto-regen Just Works), and `snapshot_applied_md_files()` walks every `*.md`. Regression coverage: `test_classify_interview_prep` (asserts label + sort-order tail position), `test_internal_prep_groups_marked_for_your_eyes_only` extended to assert the "For your eyes only" phrasing, the workflow-ordering test extended to lock Interview Prep as the ninth section, and the cross-display-name parametrize gains a `"Gamma Interview Prep - Acme - Director - 20260514-101515.md"` case. Truncation (the other half of the #666 feedback report — generated `.md` ending mid-content) tracked separately on the same issue; not in this PR. No schema change, no migration.
- **#210 feat(web): in-browser editing for generated `.md` files with auto-`.docx` regeneration.** Adds `POST /materials/{fingerprint}/files/{filename}` (`src/findajob/web/routes/materials.py`) so operators can polish AI-generated resume / cover / briefing markdown without leaving the browser. Validation: folder resolves via `folder_resolver.resolve_folder()` (path-traversal guard already enforced upstream), filename matches an entry in `_GROUP_RULES`, extension is `.md`, the filename is NOT a snapshot or `.bak` (those are read-only audit artifacts), and `jobs.stage != 'prep_in_progress'` (409 — the prep subprocess may `rmtree` the folder mid-save). Save flow: one-shot `{file}.bak` snapshot before the first edit per file; if the file classifies as a Resume, `_linkify_contact_info()` re-applies to keep email + LinkedIn URLs clickable after manual edits; atomic write via `tempfile.mkstemp` + `os.replace`; the sibling `.docx` is then regenerated via the new `findajob.prep.docx_render.render_md_to_docx()` helper. Pandoc failure after the `.md` write surfaces in the `_save_result.html` partial (reused from `/config/`) — the `.md` is still saved so user input is never lost on a pandoc transient. On the apply transition, `_move_folder_to_applied()` in `routes/board_actions.py` now calls `findajob.actions.snapshot_applied_md_files()` which walks the moved folder and copies every `*.md` to a `{name}.applied-{YYYY-MM-DD}.md` sibling — captures the as-sent state at the moment the job was submitted. Idempotent (re-applying same day is a no-op); no retroactive backfill for jobs already in an applied stage at deploy time. Snapshot and `.bak` files are filtered out of the per-folder UI (`_group_files`) so the Resume / Cover groups don't accumulate visible rows after every apply cycle — they remain on disk for audit. `POST_APPLIED_STAGES` (`applied`, `interview`, `offer`, `not_selected`, `withdrawn`) gates a yellow banner on the materials page: *"Already sent. Sent to the employer on YYYY-MM-DD. The original-as-sent .md files are preserved alongside the live ones as `*.applied-YYYY-MM-DD.md`. Edits here update the working copy only; they don't change what the employer received."* Edit affordance: each `.md` row in `templates/materials/folder.html` gains a ✎ Edit button next to View; clicking fetches the raw markdown via the existing `?raw=1` route, swaps the row inline to a textarea + Save / Cancel, and posts via HTMX. Pandoc invocation lives in one place now (`findajob.prep.docx_render.render_md_to_docx(md_path, docx_path, *, has_yaml_frontmatter)`) — extracted from the three call sites in `prep/orchestrator.py:371/430/475` (briefing / resume / cover); the prep flow continues to call it for its three generated documents, and the edit-and-save flow calls it for the single edited file. `has_yaml_frontmatter` is derived from `_classify_file()`: True for standard prep "Briefing", False for the speculative `briefing.md`. Two regression guards updated: `test_prep_subprocess_failure.py`'s textual `check=True` count now scans both `orchestrator.py` and `docx_render.py` (4 → 2 sites after extraction); the snapshot/`.bak` filter in `_group_files` is asserted in `test_materials_grouping.py`. Closes and consolidates #305 (filed 5 days after #210 with narrower scope — copy-MD shipped separately as #347; edit-in-place was the remaining piece).
- **#150 feat(web): `/tools/` page — guided LLM prompts for profile updates and config tuning.** Promotes the placeholder `/tools/` route (previously a two-tile stub linking to `/onboarding/?mode=rerun` and `/config/`) to a real data-driven tile registry at `src/findajob/web/tools_registry.py`. Three prompt tiles ship in this PR: **Refresh your profile** (conversational walkthrough emitting edits for `candidate_context/profile.md` sections), **Tune what gets rejected** (enforces the title-only vs JD-content locus split as the first question — title-only signals route to `config/prefilter_rules.yaml` regex hard-rejects, JD-content signals route to `profile.md` `## Excluded Categories` or `## Title Calibration Notes` — and refuses to enumerate company names or invent industry vocabulary), and **Calibrate cover-letter voice** (extracts voice patterns from a sample letter into a markdown file suitable for `candidate_context/voice_samples/`). Each prompt tile renders a **Copy prompt** button (Alpine.js + `navigator.clipboard.writeText` with graceful `.catch()` for non-secure contexts) and an **Open in Claude** anchor pointing at `https://claude.ai/new?q=<urlencoded prompt>`. The anchor is omitted when the URL-encoded prompt exceeds 6 KB (current prompts all encode to ~3.8–4.7 KB, comfortably under the cap). Prompts live as `config/tool_prompts/{slug}.md` and seed onto each stack via the existing `bundled-config/` → `$JSP_BASE/config/` flow in `ops/entrypoint.sh` — operator-editable through the `/config/` editor like any other config file. Adding a new tool = append a tile to `TILES` in `tools_registry.py` + drop a markdown file in `config/tool_prompts/`; no schema, no migration, no env var. Phase 1 scope is intentionally narrow — the design constraints captured in the 2026-04-25 brainstorm comment on #150 (mandatory per-(source × score-band) rule preview, false-negative gate against applied jobs, "explain my score-X jobs" cluster sampler) describe a future interactive rule-editor surface and are filed as a successor issue.

### Migration required

- **#658** — after `docker compose pull && docker compose up -d`, the next 30-minute `detect-rejections` cron cycle picks up new Workday / SmartRecruiters / Microsoft / Oracle rejections going forward. To **also recover the historical cohort** (messages already past `state.rejection_last_uid` that the old allowlist excluded), flip the per-stack backlog flag and restart the container so the next cycle re-runs the 30-day backlog scan with the wider allowlist. On each Gmail-configured stack: `sudo -u <stack-user> jq '.rejection_backlog_scan_complete = false' <stack-state-dir>/config/gmail_state.json > /tmp/gs.json && sudo -u <stack-user> mv /tmp/gs.json <stack-state-dir>/config/gmail_state.json && sudo -u <stack-user> docker compose -f <stack-dir>/compose.yaml restart`. Idempotent; safe to skip on stacks without Gmail configured. Stacks with no `gmail.json` (e.g., new tester stacks pre-onboarding) are a no-op until they onboard Gmail.
- **#656** — after `docker compose pull && docker compose up -d`, run the one-off backfill on each stack to fix pre-existing gmail_linkedin rows with degenerate titles: `docker exec -u 1000 <stack-container> python /app/scripts/backfill_linkedin_titles.py --dry-run` first to enumerate, then rerun without `--dry-run` to apply. The `-u 1000` is load-bearing — bare `docker exec` runs as root, which writes root-owned WAL/SHM sidecars and breaks subsequent app-user writes (entrypoint runs as PUID:PGID, default 1000:1000). Operator stack: one active candidate as of 2026-05-13 (Lambda); the second row #645 cited (DataBank) was already in stage=`rejected` so falls outside the scope. Tester stacks: zero or low single digits expected. Re-running is safe (already-fixed rows fall out of the candidates query).

Otherwise none. `config/tool_prompts/` flows through the existing bundled-config seed in `ops/entrypoint.sh` on every container start; pure `docker compose pull` followed by `docker compose up -d` is sufficient. The `/tools/` route, its template, and the nav link were already present (stub), so no nav config changes either.

## [0.24.0] — 2026-05-13

### Added
- **#643 add(ops): Fly.io as a cloud deployment target with single-volume image layout.** Adds `ops/fly.toml.example` (tracked template, region `iad`, image pinned to `ghcr.io/brockamer/findajob:v0.23.3`, one `[[mounts]]` block at `/app/state/`, `JSP_BASE=/app/state` in `[env]` so `findajob.paths.BASE` resolves to the volume root, `[http_service]` on 8090 with a `/healthz` check, `[vm]` `shared-cpu-1x` 1 GB) and `ops/fly-deploy.sh`, an idempotent wrapper that creates the Fly app + single 8 GB volume if missing, prompts only for missing secrets (`OPENROUTER_API_KEY`, `RAPIDAPI_KEY`, `NTFY_TOPIC`, `FINDAJOB_AUTH_USER`, `FINDAJOB_AUTH_PASS`, `FINDAJOB_WEB_URL` — defaults to `https://<app>.fly.dev`), runs `fly deploy`, and verifies the basic-auth gate from inside the running machine via `fly ssh console --command "python -m findajob.web.verify_auth"` (CLAUDE.md "Auth Gate Must Be Verified Post-Deploy"). Architecturally: **one image, two layouts** gated on `JSP_BASE`. Compose stacks keep `JSP_BASE=/app` with six host bind mounts at `/app/{data,logs,companies,config,candidate_context,.backups}`. Fly stacks (and any future k8s PV/PVC target) set `JSP_BASE=/app/state` and use one volume mounted at that root; `ops/entrypoint.sh` materializes the six state subdirs underneath on every container start. Compose stacks deliberately stay on bind mounts because the `/admin/stacks/` operator-mode dashboard reads cross-stack SQLite directly from host paths, host-level backups point at those paths, and direct operator inspectability (`ls`, `tail -f`, `du` on the host filesystem) is load-bearing across the multi-stack workflow. Four file changes wire this up. (1) `ops/entrypoint.sh` reads `JSP_BASE` at the top (default `/app` from Dockerfile `ENV`); a mkdir-p step before the chown loop materializes `$JSP_BASE/{data,logs,companies,config,candidate_context,.backups}` — no-op when bind mounts already populated them, the missing piece on a fresh single volume. The bundled-config seed, chown loop, and `init_db` gate all route through `$JSP_BASE`; `.backups` is added to the chown loop. (2) `src/findajob/web/app.py:default_app()` derives `COMPANIES_ROOT` and `DB_PATH` defaults from `JSP_BASE` (`${JSP_BASE}/companies`, `${JSP_BASE}/data/pipeline.db`) so single-volume deploys resolve to the right paths without per-stack env overrides. (3) `ops/fly-deploy.sh` provisions one volume (`findajob_state`, 8 GB) instead of six; `has_secret()` strips the leading whitespace + optional `* ` staged-marker that `fly secrets list` writes into column 1 before awk's column read, so already-staged and already-deployed secrets are both correctly detected and the script doesn't re-prompt. (4) `docs/operations/fly-deploy.md` — Prerequisites includes the Fly trial-org credit-card requirement; backup, resize, and cost-guide sections describe the single-volume layout. End-state for the operator: install flyctl, `fly auth login`, ensure billing is enabled on the Fly org, `cp ops/fly.toml.example ops/fly.toml` + edit the app name, `bash ops/fly-deploy.sh`, log in with basic auth. ~$3–5/mo per tenant. Real `ops/fly.toml` is gitignored alongside the per-stack rapidapi/active-sources config because it carries the chosen Fly app name (operator topology). Runbook with threat model, docker-compose→fly translation table, cost guide, backup/rollback/teardown at `docs/operations/fly-deploy.md`; one-line pointer added to `docs/operations/README.md`.

### Migration required

None. `JSP_BASE` defaults to `/app` (the existing Dockerfile `ENV`), the entrypoint's `mkdir -p` is idempotent against existing bind mounts, and `web/app.py`'s `${JSP_BASE}/companies` / `${JSP_BASE}/data/pipeline.db` defaults resolve to the same `/app/companies` / `/app/data/pipeline.db` paths compose stacks have always used. No schema, env, crontab, mount, or compose change touches existing self-hosted stacks.

## [0.23.3] — 2026-05-11

### Fixed

- **#636 fix(prep): retry fit_analyst once on empty/malformed output + Step 7 validation blocks shipment of incomplete briefings.** `run_role` catches `OpenRouterError` and returns `""` (silent recovery) — including when Perplexity `sonar-reasoning-pro` intermittently returns `content: null`. The orchestrator's `if fit_analysis:` (`src/findajob/prep/orchestrator.py:301`) was False on that empty, so the entire Fit Analysis section silently disappeared from `briefing.md`, `fit_score_avg`/`prob_score_avg` stayed None, and the dashboard cells rendered blank. `prep_complete` fired normally — no warning, no retry. Caught after operator's Nscale "Director of Lab Services" regenerate on 2026-05-11 (pipeline.jsonl logged `openrouter_failure`/`fit_analyst` right before a clean `prep_complete`). Mirror the briefing_writer retry pattern (`orchestrator.py:271`): new module-level `_fit_analysis_is_complete(text)` helper validates that text is non-empty, contains `"Fit Matrix"`, and splits on `## 🎯 Probability Assessment` into two halves each carrying at least one `:NN%` score. When that returns False after the first call, log `fit_analyst_retry` to pipeline.jsonl and call `run_role` once more. If retry also fails, fit_score_avg/prob_score_avg stay None and Step 7 validation now appends `"briefing: missing fit analysis (...)"` to `validation_failures` — the existing `prep_validation_failed` path runs (rmtree outdir, `reset_prep_to_scored`, `quick_notify`), so the operator gets a PREP FAILED ntfy and the row drops back to scored for re-flag rather than shipping an incomplete briefing. 7 new tests under `TestFitAnalysisIsComplete` cover the contract: complete passes, empty fails, None fails, missing Fit Matrix fails, missing Probability Assessment fails, no scores in either section fails. Also adds an `onboarding_voice_samples_dropped` event log at the inject() layer so the skip decision is greppable in pipeline.jsonl alongside `voice_processor_failure`. **No `migration-required`** — pure orchestrator logic; no schema/env/cron changes. Closes #636.
- **#637 fix(notify): silent-feed-failure health-check reads from adapters dict + dynamic source enumeration.** Daily health-check ntfy was false-flagging greenhouse/ashby/lever/gmail as silent feed failures every morning. Root cause: `jobs_fetched` event shape migrated around 2026-05-09→05-10 (post #410.5 adapter migration) — per-source counts moved from top-level keys into a nested `adapters: {}` dict. `health_check.py` hardcoded `SOURCE_KEYS = ("greenhouse", "ashby", "lever", "jobsapi", "gmail")` as top-level lookups; those keys are now absent from every recent event, so window-max stayed at 0 for all four → warning fired daily on healthy feeds (concrete: 2026-05-11 pipeline.jsonl entry shows `adapters={greenhouse: 4872, ashby: 1544, lever: 304, gmail: 0}`). New module-level `_extract_source_counts()` reads from the adapters dict first and falls back to legacy top-level keys (for events older than the schema migration still in the 7-day baseline window), taking max when both locations carry a count for the same source. `_detect_dead_feeds()` enumerates source names dynamically from event content — new adapters (#617 WorkdayCXS, future ones) auto-get health-check coverage. A source is "dead" only when CONFIGURED (present in window events, even at 0) AND producing zero across all window runs AND had >0 in baseline; a source absent from every window event is treated as deliberately disabled (e.g., dropped from `active_sources.txt`), not dead. 9 new tests in `tests/test_health_check_dead_feeds.py` cover all three shapes plus oscillation tolerance, dynamic enumeration, and the disabled-source guard. **No `migration-required`** — pure notify logic; no schema/env/cron changes. Closes #637.
- **#638 fix(scorer): strip markdown-bold around JSON keys + tighten prompt against asterisks/emphasis.** DeepSeek V3.2 (the model behind `config/roles/job_scorer.md`) intermittently wraps JSON keys in markdown bold despite the prompt asking for pure JSON. Three `score_validation_failed` events on 2026-05-11 (07:07-07:08 UTC) all show the same shape — `**score_status**: "scored"` or `**"relevance_score": 1` — breaking `json.loads` with `Expecting value: line 1 column 1 (char 0)`. Today's blast radius was contained: all three jobs had titles matching `_hard_reject_match()` patterns, so the auto-fallback at `scoring.py:218` scored them as 1 without routing to manual_review. The risk is latent: the same drift on a non-rejectable title (director-level role at a target company) would misroute to manual_review. Two coordinated changes: (1) prompt-side — extend `config/roles/job_scorer.md` OUTPUT FORMAT line with explicit `"No bold (**), no asterisks, no emphasis"` prohibition; (2) parser-side — `extract_json_payload` in `src/findajob/llm_parsing.py` runs a defensive anchored regex strip — `(^|[{,]\s*)\*\*"?(\w+)"?(?:\*\*)?\s*:` → `"\1":` — over the extracted text. Both observed variants normalize to proper `"key":` form. Anchor on line start or JSON delimiter prevents matching inside a JSON string value where legitimate `**` may appear as prose. 4 new tests under `TestExtractJsonPayload` cover Variant A (bold around bare keys), Variant B (bold prefix on quoted keys), mixed shape (Vantage 2026-05-11 raw), and bold inside string-value preserved. **No `migration-required`** — prompt + parser change; no schema/env/cron changes. Closes #638.
- **#639 fix(prep): raise fit_analyst `max_tokens` to 16384 + surface `finish_reason` on null content.** Surfaced 2026-05-11 via operator's OpenRouter activity-log read of three failing fit_analyst generations (one Apple morning auto-prep at 05:07 PT plus two Nscale regenerates at 11:07 and 11:31 PT). Concrete numbers from the third generation: `native_tokens_prompt=18377`, `native_tokens_completion=4096` (hit cap exactly), `native_tokens_reasoning=4712`, `finish_reason="length"`, `content=null`. Perplexity `sonar-reasoning-pro` is a reasoning model that spends "reasoning tokens" before emitting content; the openrouter wrapper's `DEFAULT_MAX_TOKENS=4096` cap was insufficient — the model exhausted the entire output budget on internal reasoning before reaching the actual fit-matrix output. Same failure mode as #632 (onboarding voice-samples emit hit 4096 cap on Sonnet); same fix shape: add `max_tokens: 16384` to `config/roles/fit_analyst.md` frontmatter. Sonar-reasoning-pro supports up to 200K context so 16384 is well within model limits. Operator verified end-to-end after deploy: re-regenerated Nscale Director of Lab Services; prep succeeded; briefing now contains populated Fit Matrix + Probability Assessment sections; dashboard cells render scores. Also enriches the `OpenRouterError` raised on null content to include `finish_reason` — pipeline.jsonl now logs `"Content not a string: NoneType; finish_reason=length"` instead of just `"Content not a string: NoneType"`, making the budget-exhausted case immediately diagnosable without an external dashboard lookup. Defensive: future content-null cases on other roles surface the cause inline. Note: `company_researcher.md` and `company_discoverer.md` use the same Perplexity reasoning model but DID NOT receive the bump — both produce non-empty output today (briefings exist, weekly discoverer file produced), so they're not at the edge of the 4096 cap; bumping them preemptively would raise cost ceilings without confirmed need. Will revisit if either fails the same way later. Cost note: per-prep cost rose to ~$3 after this bump; investigation deferred (see #640 follow-up). **No `migration-required`** — frontmatter edit + diagnostic enhancement; no schema/env/cron changes. Closes #639.

## [0.23.2] — 2026-05-11

### Fixed

- **#621 fix(onboarding): lock interviewer option-prefix style to letters, forbid digits and bullets.** Beta tester walking through fresh-install NUX on 2026-05-10 saw the onboarding interviewer LLM mix `a. b. c.`, `1. 2. 3.`, and `- foo` formats across questions in the same session, having to re-figure the reply convention every time. Root cause: the meta-rule at `config/roles/onboarding_interviewer.md:30-34` literally instructed the LLM to "prefix each with a letter (a, b, c, …) **or** digit (1, 2, 3, …)" — the optionality let the model pick a different style per question, and bullets snuck in on long lists where the model defaulted to its training-prior list style. Issue body recommended switching to digits, but the prompt's downstream architecture treats sub-phase 3g's `a/b/c` as semantic identifiers mapping to RapidAPI / company-feeds / Gmail-alerts source selection (referenced in ~12 places across Phases 3-5, plus Group `a/b/c/d` framing for emit groups). Switching to digits would cascade into rewriting all of that. Instead, lock to letters — every actual question in the prompt already uses them — and explicitly prohibit the other two styles in the meta-rule. Rewritten meta-rule names letters, explicitly forbids digits + bullets, and tells the LLM "One style across every question in the session — testers got confused when a list switched format mid-interview (#621)." 3 new static invariant tests in `tests/test_onboarding_role_prompt_invariants.py` lock the contract: (a) no `letter ... or ... digit` proximity in the file (guards against the original optionality returning), (b) "Letter every list of options" heading present, (c) explicit `Do NOT use (digits|bullets)` prohibition. **Empirical end-to-end verification is operator territory** — requires a fresh interview run on `findajob-clean` post-deploy with the factory-reset procedure (`docs/personal/findajob-clean-reset.md`). The static invariants ensure the prompt source is correct; the actual LLM behavior on the new prompt is observable only by running it. **No `migration-required`** — pure prompt change; no schema/env/cron changes. Closes #621.
- **#632 fix(onboarding): voice-samples emit truncated at ~17.7K chars under prior 4096-token cap; raise to 16384 + detect length-finish.** Onboarding interview's emit phase reads back the user's voice-samples body verbatim under a `<<<FILE: voice-samples.md>>>` wrapper. With `max_tokens: 4096` in `config/roles/onboarding_interviewer.md` frontmatter, Claude Sonnet 4.6 capped that response at ~17.7K chars (4096 × ~4.3 chars/token), cutting the emit mid-block; the parser then silently didn't capture the unterminated block, `finalize_ready` stayed False, and the user clicked Finalize to a confusing "still missing voice-samples.md" error with no actionable signal. Reported by external tester in #624 comment 2026-05-11T06:55Z across two separate runs; reproduced by inspection (4096-token math matches the observed truncation boundary). Three coordinated changes: (1) `config/roles/onboarding_interviewer.md` frontmatter `max_tokens: 4096` → `16384` — fits ~57K chars of output comfortably (Claude Sonnet 4.6 supports 64K output tokens, so further headroom remains). `findajob.onboarding.interview_runner.INTERVIEW_MAX_TOKENS` constant bumped to match. (2) `findajob.llm.openrouter.CompletionResult` gains a `finish_reason: str | None = None` field; `_parse_response` extracts `data["choices"][0].finish_reason` (OpenAI/OpenRouter standard shape). Default-None keeps every existing `CompletionResult(...)` construction site (8 across tests) working without changes. (3) `findajob.onboarding.interview_runner.run_turn` checks `result.finish_reason == "length"` after the `complete()` call and raises `InterviewRunnerError(kind="length", ...)` via `_translate` with a clear "your input is too long for a single emit; trim the longest block (usually voice samples) and try again" recovery message. The route already renders `InterviewRunnerError.user_message` verbatim in the chat banner — no route change needed. 6 new tests: 3 in `tests/test_llm_openrouter.py` covering `finish_reason` extraction (`stop`, `length`, missing→None); 3 in `tests/test_onboarding_interview_runner.py` for max_tokens floor, length-detection raise, and that `stop`/missing finish_reason don't raise spuriously. Updated existing `test_interview_max_tokens_is_4096` to `test_interview_max_tokens_supports_voice_samples_emit` asserting `>= 16384`. **No `migration-required`** — pure prompt/wrapper change; no schema/env/cron changes; existing onboarding sessions in-flight will pick up the bump on next turn (the role file is read fresh per call). Closes #632.
- **#635 fix(web): speculative status/review pages 500'd on every render after #618 — module-local Jinja templates instance had no globals.** Filed and started as a test-only bug (7 tests in `tests/test_speculative_routes.py` failing with `UndefinedError: 'onboarding_complete' is undefined`). Scope expanded during context-load: `src/findajob/web/routes/speculative.py:34` declared its own module-local `templates = Jinja2Templates(...)` instance — every other route module (config, tools, ingest, onboarding, materials, settings_active_sources, …) renders via `request.app.state.templates` which `findajob.web.app.create_app` populates with ~10 Jinja globals. The module-local instance had none of those globals registered, so when #618 (merged 2026-05-10) added `{% if onboarding_complete(request) %}` to `_nav.html`, every full-page speculative render started raising `UndefinedError` — both in tests and in production. Speculative is cold-outreach (M6 / #131-B3 path); the operator's stack just hadn't clicked through a `/speculative/status/{id}` or `/speculative/review/{id}` page since #618 shipped, so the production 500 stayed dormant until the #631 full-suite run surfaced the tests. Fix: delete `speculative.py`'s module-local templates declaration and the `Jinja2Templates` import; refactor the 3 `templates.TemplateResponse(...)` call sites (`get_status`, `poll_status`, `get_review` at lines 136/153/176) to `request.app.state.templates.TemplateResponse(...)` — aligns speculative with every other route module and eliminates the global-leak surface entirely. Test fixture `_make_app` in `test_speculative_routes.py` switched from bare `FastAPI() + include_router(speculative.router)` to `create_app(...)` so the test rig exercises the same templates path as production (the prior minimal rig was test-only and would have kept hiding this class of bug indefinitely). `app.state.onboarding_complete=True` bypasses the guard so the tests stay scoped to speculative behavior. Module-local `DB_PATH` override preserved — eventual cleanup to `app.state.db_path` deferred. **No `migration-required`** — pure web behavior fix; no schema/env/cron changes; production stacks need only `docker compose pull && up -d` to pick it up. Closes #635.
- **#631 fix(onboarding): graceful 402 PaymentRequired + transactional finalize emit.** When OpenRouter returned 402 during the onboarding interview's Finalize step (out-of-credit account), the route returned a generic 400 Bad Request and the captured config files were committed to disk *before* the smoke-check verified the key. After a credit top-up the interview agent rejoined a dirty state — `/onboarding/feed-config/` 500s on the half-seeded layout, blank profile.md, etc. (spun off from #624's external-tester reproducer). Fix has three coordinated pieces. (1) `OnboardingSmokeCheckFailed` now carries a `status_code` attribute (default 400; injector sets 402 when `verify_openrouter_key`'s error message contains "402 Payment Required") — `src/findajob/onboarding/openrouter_smoke.py`. (2) The smoke check in `inject()` moved BEFORE the `os.replace` commit loop (was after). The existing rollback path (delete every staged tempfile + the backup dir created this run) now handles `OnboardingSmokeCheckFailed` too — previously that branch deliberately preserved committed files for a paste-back retry, but that strategy was the source of the blank-file bug. Updated docstring at `inject()`'s top spells out the new contract — `src/findajob/onboarding/injector.py`. (3) `/onboarding/interview/{sid}/finalize` reads `e.status_code` off the exception and renders with the matching code (402 with "Once credits land, return here and click Finalize again — no config files were written" copy; 400 keeps the legacy "OpenRouter rejected the key" framing for 401/429/network) — `src/findajob/web/routes/onboarding_interview.py`. Six new regression tests in `tests/test_onboarding_finalize_402.py`: status_code carried on the exception, injector raises 402 on payment-required message, no config files survive a failed smoke check (the all-or-nothing AC), route surfaces HTTP 402, no partial files via the route path, and the resume-after-top-up flow (first call 402 → second call 303 with files committed). Pre-existing `test_inject_smoke_check_failure_raises_and_skips_sentinel` renamed to `_raises_and_rolls_back` and its files-exist assertions inverted to match the new transactional contract. `docs/troubleshooting.md` carries a new "Onboarding finalize fails with 402 PaymentRequired" symptom-index entry describing the recovery flow. **No `migration-required`** — pure web/onboarding behavior change; no schema/env/cron changes; existing fully-onboarded stacks unaffected. Closes #631.
- **#628 fix(web,obs): route-raised `HTTPException(>=500)` now surfaces in `pipeline.jsonl`.** Previously a route handler raising `HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="...")` returned the detail to the client but wrote nothing server-side — uvicorn's access log shows only `500 Internal Server Error` and the operator has to replay the request and inspect the response body to learn what blew up (surfaced 2026-05-11 while triaging #624's feed-config 500 — `"Curation file not found: ..."` was invisible in `docker logs`). New `@app.exception_handler(HTTPException)` in `findajob.web.app.create_app` writes `log_event("http_5xx", path=..., status=..., detail=...)` for `status_code >= 500` then delegates rendering to FastAPI's default `http_exception_handler`. Client-error 4xx skip the log entirely (no traceback spam). Three regression tests in `tests/test_web_5xx_logging.py` lock the contract: 500 logs structured event, 503 logs with correct status/detail, 404 logs nothing. **No `migration-required`** — purely additive observability; route handler behavior and response shapes unchanged. Closes #628.
- **#629 fix(web,a11y): duplicate `<h1>` on `/onboarding/gmail-config/` and asymmetric heading on `/config/gmail/`.** `gmail_config/_card.html` declared `<h1 class="text-2xl font-bold">Gmail Job Alert Ingestion</h1>` which collided with the wrapper `<h1>` at `src/findajob/web/templates/onboarding_gmail_config/index.html:16` ("Set up Gmail job-alert ingestion") — two top-level headings on one page, screen readers announce both. The other includer `gmail_config/index.html` (the `/config/gmail/` wrapper) had no page-level heading of its own — its only top-level heading came from the card. Demoting `_card.html`'s `<h1>` → `<h2>` in isolation would have left `/config/gmail/` with zero top-level headings (swap one a11y bug for another). Fix: demote `_card.html`'s `<h1>` → `<h2>` (the card is a section inside each wrapper) and add a page-level `<h1>Gmail integration</h1>` to `gmail_config/index.html`. Both paths now render exactly one `<h1>` (confirmed via static template chain analysis: `base.html` + `_nav.html` contribute zero headings). **No `migration-required`** — pure template change; no schema/env/cron changes. Closes #629.
- **#627 — `/onboarding/feed-config/{sid}` no longer 500s on fresh installs.** New `findajob.config_seed.seed_runtime_config` helper invoked from `ops/entrypoint.sh` at every container start: if `config/rapidapi_feeds.yaml` is absent, copy from the bundled `rapidapi_feeds.yaml.example`. Idempotent — operator edits survive restarts. Mirrors the `init_db.py` pattern (small Python module, shell entrypoint dispatches). No `### Migration required`: existing stacks where the operator already produced `rapidapi_feeds.yaml` are unaffected; stacks where the file was missing (the bug shape) auto-heal on next `docker compose pull && up -d`.
- **#626 fix(onboarding): `finalize_ready` checks required-set membership, not total cardinality.** External tester surfaced via #624 that the chat UI's emit counter read "13 of 10 required blocks captured" — past the threshold, but Finalize still blocked. Root cause: `finalize_ready` compared `len(captured)` against `len(ALLOWED_FILENAMES)` rather than verifying that every required filename was present. Optional emissions (`voice-samples.md`, `jsearch_queries.txt`, `feed-urls.txt`, `linkedin-alerts.md`, `target_locations.txt`, `rapidapi_feed.txt`) inflated the count past 10 while a required block was still missing, so the user clicked Finalize and got a cryptic "still missing X" error. Fix is a one-line membership check: `all(name in captured for name in ALLOWED_FILENAMES)`. Two regression tests in `tests/test_onboarding_interview_runner.py` lock the contract: extra optional emissions don't unblock when required are missing, and the happy path where required are complete still returns True. **No `migration-required`** — pure logic fix; no schema/env/cron changes. Closes #626.
- **#634 fix(onboarding): voice-samples LLM redact failure silently writes unredacted PII to disk.** Discovered while implementing #631: `inject()` called `process_voice_samples()` and unpacked the redaction-success flag into `_redaction_ok` (ignored), then guarded the write on body truthiness. On `OpenRouterError`, `process_voice_samples` returns `(cleaned, False)` where `cleaned` is the structurally-cleaned but NOT-LLM-redacted body — still carrying every verbatim full name, employer, and locale the user pasted. The truthy check passed; unredacted content landed at `candidate_context/voice_samples/voice-samples.md` and was loaded into every downstream materials prompt (resume tailor, cover letter, briefing, recruiter critique, outreach drafter). Fix: honor the `redaction_ok` flag explicitly. When False, skip staging the tempfile entirely, log `onboarding_voice_samples_dropped` to `pipeline.jsonl`, and set a new `InjectResult.voice_samples_redact_failed` flag. The `finalize_interview` route appends `?voice_redact_failed=1` to the post-finalize redirect; both feed-config and gmail-config landing pages render an amber banner pointing the operator at `/onboarding/?mode=rerun`. New shared partial `templates/onboarding/_voice_redact_failed_banner.html`. 4 new tests in `tests/test_onboarding_injector.py` (redact-failure path skips write + flag set, empty-after-cleaning still has flag False, success path has flag False, no-voice-samples path has flag False); 4 new route tests across `tests/test_onboarding_gmail_config_route.py` and `tests/test_onboarding_feed_config_route.py` (banner renders with query param, absent without). Existing optional-file machinery (`_OPTIONAL_DESTINATIONS` skip-when-absent) did the heavy lifting — no new conditional branch in the transactional commit/rollback loop. **No `migration-required`** — pure web/onboarding behavior fix; no schema/env/cron changes. Closes #634.

## [0.23.1] — 2026-05-10

### Migration required

- **Operator-side stack rename + new staging stack standup.** The factory-fresh stack must be renamed `findajob-test` → `findajob-clean` (atomic stack-dir rename plus compose tag rename — see prior tester-stack rename precedent for the procedure). The new `findajob-staging` stack must be stood up on `<deployment-host>` per the operator-private setup doc, with HTTP Basic Auth + `python -m findajob.web.verify_auth` post-deploy (CLAUDE.md hard rule).
- **Operator-side first reset.** After staging stack standup, run `docker exec -u 1000 findajob-staging-scheduler-1 python -m findajob.staging.reset` to copy the persona fixture into bind mounts.
- **Operator-side staging cron flips.** Set `FINDAJOB_STAGING_{PREP,INTERVIEW,SPECULATIVE,ADVANCE}_ENABLED=true` in staging's `.env`. Other stacks leave them unset (default disabled).
- **No schema migration required.** This change is pure tier expansion; no DB columns added, no rows changed on existing stacks.

### Added

- **#617 feat(fetchers): WorkdayCXSAdapter — direct Workday CXS API ingestion.** Adds Workday as a first-class job source under the `JobSourceAdapter` Protocol established in #410.1–#410.5, closing the F500/large-enterprise coverage gap (Workday is the dominant ATS for Salesforce, NVIDIA, Citi, Twilio, JPM, and many others). Phase 1 (#248) characterized the request shape — naive payload `{"appliedFacets":{},"limit":20,"offset":0,"searchText":""}` returns 200, no API key, no warm-up GET, no CSRF. New `src/findajob/fetchers/adapters/workday_cxs.py` parses tenant URLs from `config/feed_urls.txt` via the regex `https?://([^./?#]+)\.(wd\d+)\.myworkdayjobs\.com/([^/?#]+)` (captures tenant, pod, site as a 3-tuple); same first-occurrence-wins dedupe pattern as Greenhouse/Ashby/Lever, except the dedup key omits pod so a tenant migrating wd5 → wd12 doesn't double-count during the migration window. `fetch()` paginates the list endpoint via `offset` and follows up with one detail GET per posting (Workday's list response is summary-only — JD body lives in `jobPostingInfo.jobDescription`). Hard cap at `_PER_TENANT_CAP=500` postings per tenant per cycle bounds wall-clock time on a runaway tenant (Workday returns up to 2000 per tenant; real active counts are usually 100-500). 0.5s sleep between detail fetches (2 req/sec budget; #248 Phase 1 observed no 429 at 1 req/sec). HTML JD preserved at fetch time per Greenhouse pattern; downstream pipeline strips tags. Company name falls back to tenant slug — `hiringOrganization.name` returns Workday legal-entity codes ("2100 NVIDIA USA") which are worse than the slug for display. `live_test()` is list-only and returns the standard `LiveTestBucket` set (success / zero_rows / auth on 404 / rate_limit on 429 / server on 5xx / network on RequestException / auth when no tenants configured). Registered in `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS` (`registry.py`) but **not** in `_DEFAULT_ACTIVE_SOURCES` — opt-in only per the post-#410.5 convention (operator enables via `/settings/active-sources/`). `JobSourceAdapter` Protocol conformance (#512) and `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS` membership (#516) invariants auto-include the new adapter and pass without modification. 21 new tests in `tests/test_workday_cxs_adapter.py` covering: `is_configured` (3 cases), tenant extraction (6 cases including numeric site IDs like Citi's `2`, multi-pod variants, dedup including the wd5→wd12 migration case, ignoring non-Workday URLs), `fetch()` (5 cases including normalized rows, missing externalPath, detail 404, list 500, `_PER_TENANT_CAP` enforcement), `live_test()` (7 cases, one per `LiveTestBucket` value plus the no-tenants-configured branch). `docs/architecture/file-map.md` adapter line updated. **No `migration-required`** — additive opt-in, no schema/env/cron changes; existing stacks unaffected. Closes #617.

- **#616 feat(materials): Regenerate button on the per-job materials page.** Materials hand-review (e.g., the #259 cover-letter complementarity loop) previously required navigating back to the dashboard, finding the row, and using the Regenerate dropdown — high friction during side-by-side compare. New action panel in `templates/materials/folder.html` (between the Google-Docs workflow helper and the document groups) shows the last-generated timestamp from `jobs.stage_updated`, rendered client-side via `Date.toLocaleString` so it lands in the operator's local time. Click reveals an Alpine.js confirm step that explicitly warns existing materials will be deleted (resume, cover, briefing, recruiter critique, outreach drafts), then a regular form POST to `/materials/{fingerprint}/regenerate`. Backend at `src/findajob/web/routes/materials.py` mirrors the dashboard handler's gates (404 / idempotent on `prep_in_progress` / 303 to `/materials/?regen_error=queue_full` when `_prep_in_flight >= MAX_CONCURRENT_PREPS`); the materials index template surfaces the queue-full banner. The actual side-effect sequence (folder rmtree, stage flip to `prep_in_progress`, audit row, pipeline event, `_launch_prep_subprocess`) is shared via a new `board_actions._execute_regenerate` helper so the dashboard and materials handlers can't drift apart. The new pipeline event name `web_regen_dispatched_from_materials` distinguishes the source. When `stage='prep_in_progress'`, the button is replaced with a disabled "Regenerating…" pill — matches the existing handler's idempotency contract. Four new tests in `tests/test_board_actions.py::TestRegenerateFromMaterials` (happy path redirects + dispatches, 404, idempotent on in-progress, queue-full redirect with error param). **No `migration-required`** — additive route, no schema/env/cron changes. Closes #616.

- **#571 feat(onboarding,ui): connections.csv upload step (fresh-install path).** New terminal onboarding step at `/onboarding/connections/{session_id}/` prompts the user to upload their LinkedIn Connections.csv export — the input that drives `findajob.find_contacts` for outreach drafting. Previously the file was silently expected at `state/data/connections.csv` with no UI on-ramp; a fresh-install tester would never know it existed. New route in `src/findajob/web/routes/onboarding_connections.py` (GET render + POST upload + POST skip) and template `templates/onboarding_connections/index.html` carrying the LinkedIn-export procedure (Settings → Data Privacy → Get a copy of your data → Connections), strict CSV-header validation against the six columns `findajob.find_contacts` reads, atomic write via tempfile + `os.replace`, UTF-8-sig decoding to swallow LinkedIn's occasional BOM, an explicit Notes-preamble rejection with how-to-fix copy, and a 16 MiB ceiling. Both Upload (header-valid CSV accepted) and Skip write the sentinel and redirect to `/board/dashboard`. Sentinel-write responsibility moved from `/onboarding/gmail-config/{sid}/{skip,finish}` to the new connections gate; gmail-config's `/finish` preserves its IMAP-test-before-handoff guarantee from #407 unchanged. Adjacent test files updated (`test_onboarding_gmail_config_route.py`, `test_onboarding_feed_config_route.py`, `test_onboarding_injector.py`, `test_onboarding_interview_integration.py`) to reflect the new chain. New `tests/test_onboarding_connections_route.py` (7 tests) covers GET render with explainer, Skip happy path, Upload happy path with atomic write + sentinel, header-missing-column rejection, LinkedIn `Notes:` preamble rejection with how-to-fix message, empty-file rejection, and the UTF-8 BOM passthrough. **Trimmed scope per 2026-05-10 start-time backstop**: the `/settings/connections/` refresh page (last-imported date, row count, refresh, remove) from the full issue body was deferred to #614 to ship the fresh-install path same-day for a tester walkthrough. **No `migration-required`** — additive route, no schema/env/cron changes; existing stacks unaffected.
- **#565 dev pipeline: introduce `findajob-staging`; rename `findajob-test` → `findajob-clean`.** Three named application tiers (`findajob-clean` / `findajob-staging` / `<operator-stack>`) replace the prior two-stack ad-hoc pre-cohort gate. Newly-tracked code: `src/findajob/staging/{clicker,green,reset}.py` (image-baked CLI modules), `src/findajob/staging/persona_fixture/` (deterministic Jordan Riley persona + config), four staging-only entries in `ops/scheduled-jobs.yaml` (default `enabled: false`). New release-process step: `python -m findajob.staging.green` exits 0 before any tag cut. Spec at `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-08-565-dev-pipeline-design.md` (gitignored). Closes #565 once one full release ships through the new gate end-to-end.

### Changed

- **#259 cover_letter_writer: consume tailored resume for complementarity (not consistency).** The cover_letter_writer LLM call previously built its draft from `cached_prefix=shared_with_voice` (profile + master_resume + JD + voice_samples) plus a variable suffix carrying only `mode_marker + Date + COMPANY BRIEFING AND FIT ANALYSIS`. The tailored resume produced by the immediately-prior `resume_tailor` stage was not visible to the cover letter writer, so the model had to guess what the resume emphasized and hope its cover letter picked a different angle. Common failure mode: resume leads with story A, cover letter opens with story B — disjoint narrative — or the cover letter recites resume bullets in prose form, wasting high-value real estate. Fix at `src/findajob/prep/orchestrator.py:419-433` — `cover_prompt` now appends `TAILORED RESUME:\n{resume_md}` to the variable portion (NOT the cached prefix; `resume_md` is per-job and would bust the Anthropic prompt cache for every prep). New `## RELATIONSHIP TO TAILORED RESUME` section at the top of `config/roles/cover_letter_writer.md` frames the resume's role as *facts established*, the cover letter's role as *complementary narrative the resume can't carry* — motivation, voice, why-now/why-this-company — with explicit prohibition on recital phrases ("as you can see on my resume"). Forward constraint for #496 (big-idea, prep LLM parallelization): this change introduces a serialization edge `cover_letter_writer → resume_tailor` that didn't previously exist; #496 must preserve this dependency if activated. **No `migration-required`** — pure prompt change; existing prep folders unaffected. Closes #259.

### Fixed
- **#618 fix(web,onboarding): nav notifications-badge HTMX poll infinite-loops during onboarding.** Fresh-install testers couldn't proceed past `/onboarding/` — the `_nav.html` notifications-badge polling element (`<span hx-get="/notifications/badge" hx-trigger="load, every 60s" hx-swap="outerHTML">`) hit the guarded notifications router, which 307s to `/onboarding/`. HTMX followed the redirect and `outerHTML`-swapped the entire onboarding page body into the badge slot; the injected nav's `load` trigger fired again, producing a tight loop in container logs (alternating `/onboarding/ 200` + `/notifications/badge 307`) and a corrupted UI carrying an entire injected HTML document inside the nav. Cache hid it from anyone already past onboarding: the guard caches `app.state.onboarding_complete=True` after the first authenticated hit, so operator/staging/clean stacks short-circuit and never see the redirect — only fresh installs (testers, factory-reset findajob-clean) exercise it. Fix extracts a reusable `onboarding_complete(request) -> bool` predicate out of `require_onboarding_complete` in `src/findajob/web/onboarding_guard.py`; `src/findajob/web/app.py` registers it as a Jinja global; `src/findajob/web/templates/_nav.html` wraps the entire notifications `<li>` (bell link + badge poll) with `{% if onboarding_complete(request) %}`. Post-onboarding behavior unchanged. Parametrized regression test in `tests/test_web_onboarding_guard.py` asserts the polling element is absent on `/onboarding/`, `/tools/`, `/docs/`, `/config/` pre-onboarding and present on `/board/dashboard` post-onboarding — locks the contract that no ungated HTML page polls a guarded endpoint. **No `migration-required`** — template/global change only; existing stacks unaffected. Closes #618.
- **#497 fix(find_contacts): word-boundary regex in `company_match()`.** `findajob.find_contacts.company_match()` matched after suffix-strip with raw `s in c or c in s`, so "Apple" matched "GreenApple Inc." and short tokens like "AI" matched anything containing "ai" anywhere ("AIRBUS", "Maine startups"). Surfaced false-positive contacts in outreach drafts. Match step replaced with bidirectional word-boundary regex `re.search(rf"\b{re.escape(needle)}\b", haystack)` — boundaries reject prefix collisions ("Apple" no longer matches inside "GreenApple") and substring tokens ("AI" no longer matches inside "AIRBUS"). Hyphens and dots count as non-word characters, so "Coca-Cola" still matches itself and "OpenAI" stays distinct from "Open". Blank-string guard from CLAUDE.md §"company_match() Discipline" preserved verbatim. CLAUDE.md section title renamed (singular "Blank String Guard" → "Discipline") and now codifies both rules — blank-string guard + word-boundary matching — so future re-implementations can't regress to substring `in`. Six new tests in `tests/test_find_contacts.py` covering blank guard, legitimate suffix-stripped matches, prefix-collision rejection, short-string rejection, hyphen/dot handling, and multi-word companies. AC4 spot-check on the operator's stack `_applied/` (134 outreach files across all folders, sampled most-recent batch): all observed contact-company pairings are correct — bug regression risk was real but hadn't surfaced in recent target companies. **No `migration-required`** — pure logic change; existing prep folders unaffected. Closes #497.
- **#495 fix(prep): surface silent `prep_application.py` subprocess failures.** The 4 must-succeed subprocesses inside `findajob.prep.orchestrator._run_prep` (3× pandoc `.md→.docx`, 1× `scripts/find_contacts.py`) ran with `check=False`, so a non-zero exit produced a partial materials folder while stage advanced to `materials_drafted` and the operator got a "Drafts ready" ntfy — silent application-rate suppression. All 4 sites now use `check=True, capture_output=True`; `_run_prep`'s body is wrapped in a `try/except subprocess.CalledProcessError` that calls a new `_handle_prep_subprocess_failure` helper. On failure the helper writes a `.failed_subprocess` sentinel into the prep folder (cmd / returncode / stderr tail), emits a `prep_subprocess_failed` event to `pipeline.jsonl`, calls `reset_prep_to_scored` (which writes `audit_log` and a `prep_failed_reset` event), sends a "PREP FAILED (subprocess)" ntfy, and re-raises as `SystemExit(1)`. The partial folder is preserved (not `rmtree`-ed like the existing validation-failure path) so the operator can inspect what got produced before it died. Advisory subprocesses (curl/pandoc JD-fetch fallback at L141-149, `validate_resume.py` informational quality check) intentionally stay on `check=False` because their failures are not pipeline-blocking. New `tests/test_prep_subprocess_failure.py` (7 tests) covers the handler's stage rollback, audit_log row, sentinel write, pipeline event, no-advance-to-materials_drafted, missing-outdir best-effort fallback, and a mechanical regex-guard that the 4 must-succeed sites carry `check=True`. **No `migration-required`** — failure-path-only behavior change; existing successful preps unaffected. Closes #495.

## [0.23.0] — 2026-05-09

### Migration required
- **#410.5: stacks with an explicit `config/active_sources.txt` must add the four formerly-unconditional adapter names.** Pre-#410.5 the orchestrator fired `fetch_greenhouse_jobs` / `fetch_ashby_jobs` / `fetch_lever_jobs` / `fetch_gmail_jobs` *unconditionally* alongside the registry loop — so `active_sources.txt` only ever gated the RapidAPI adapters (`jobs-api14`, `jobs-api14-indeed`, `jsearch`). After #410.5 every adapter is registry-gated. Stacks whose existing `active_sources.txt` looks like `jobs-api14\njsearch` (the operator's stack and the early NUX wave testers' stacks) need to add `greenhouse`, `ashby`, `lever`, `gmail` (whichever apply) before deploying or those sources go silent. **Stacks with no `active_sources.txt`** at all are unaffected — the `_DEFAULT_ACTIVE_SOURCES` constant expanded from `["jobs-api14"]` to all 7 registered adapter names, preserving the pre-cutover effective default surface (every adapter that `is_configured()` returns True for). **Verification** post-deploy on each stack: `sqlite3 state/data/pipeline.db "SELECT source, COUNT(*) FROM jobs WHERE created_at > datetime('now', '-7 days') GROUP BY source"` pre-deploy and ~24h post-deploy; same source labels in same proportions = behavior preserved (AC #5 of #410). If a source disappears post-deploy, add it to that stack's `active_sources.txt` and re-trigger triage.

### Changed
- **#410.5 refactor(triage): orchestrator iterates registry only; delete `fetch_jobsapi_jobs` dead code; close #410 epic.** Final sub-PR of the #410 fetcher-adapter-migration epic (#591/#410.1, #597/#410.2, #598/#410.3, #599/#410.4 preceded it). `findajob/triage/orchestrator.py:100-138` collapses from a dual-fetch block (four `fetch_*_jobs` wrapper calls + a `iter_configured_adapters()` loop) to a single registry loop — every adapter gets the same `queries` list, board-feed adapters ignore it via `del queries`. The `gmail_since_days` diagnostic-flag plumbing (CLI `--gmail-since-days`) is handled with a single in-loop swap (`if adapter.name == "gmail" and gmail_since_days is not None: adapter = GmailLinkedInAdapter(since_days=...)`) — the Protocol stays uniform across adapters, the registry stays kwarg-free, and the diagnostic path doesn't double-fetch gmail. The four thin function-style wrappers (`fetch_greenhouse_jobs`, `fetch_ashby_jobs`, `fetch_lever_jobs`, `fetch_gmail_jobs`) #410.1-4 left in place during transition are deleted from `findajob/fetchers/__init__.py`. Long-dead `fetch_jobsapi_jobs(queries_path)` (replaced by `JobsApi14Adapter` in #408) plus its orphaned `_date_posted_for_install` helper and `_NEW_INSTALL_DAYS` constant deleted from `__init__.py` — the live `_date_posted_for_install` continues to live at `findajob.fetchers.adapters.jobs_api14:261` where `JobsApi14Adapter.fetch()` calls it. Now-unused `os` and `typing.Any` imports dropped from `__init__.py`. `_DEFAULT_ACTIVE_SOURCES` in `findajob/fetchers/adapters/registry.py` expanded from `["jobs-api14"]` to all 7 registered adapter names — see Migration required above. `_gmail_disclosure.html` doc-link updated from `src/findajob/fetchers.py:fetch_gmail_jobs` to `src/findajob/fetchers/adapters/gmail.py:GmailLinkedInAdapter`. `jobs_fetched` log_event schema simplified: dropped the per-source named fields (`greenhouse=`, `ashby=`, `lever=`, `gmail=`); the canonical post-#410 form is `adapters={name: count, ...}` which scales to any registered adapter. **Operator dashboards / pipeline.jsonl analysis tools that parse the named fields need updating to read from the `adapters` dict.** `tests/test_fetchers_date_posted.py` updated to import from `findajob.fetchers.adapters.jobs_api14` and patch `findajob.paths.BASE` (lazy import in the function means the canonical paths-module attr is the right patch target). `tests/test_active_sources_parser.py` updated default-value assertions to use the `_DEFAULT_ACTIVE_SOURCES` constant rather than the hardcoded pre-#410.5 list. `tests/test_adapter_registry.py::test_iter_configured_adapters_default_when_file_missing` updated: with the expanded default and only `JOBS_API14_KEY` set, both `jobs-api14` and `jobs-api14-indeed` get yielded (per #414 they share the key). Closes #410 (the parent Epic). The four direct-fetcher follow-ups (#248 Workday CXS, #249 Gem GraphQL, future Indeed-direct, #422 JobsApi14BingAdapter) are filed against the framework directly when they land — no further orchestrator changes needed.
- **#410.4 feat(fetchers): `GmailLinkedInAdapter` — migrate `fetch_gmail_jobs` to JobSourceAdapter framework (IMAP-backed, dynamic source label).** Fourth of five sub-PRs implementing the #410 Epic. The most idiosyncratic of the four migrations: IMAP-backed (no env var, no slug pattern), the only adapter where per-row `source` is set dynamically (`gmail_linkedin` / `gmail_indeed` / `gmail_ziprecruiter` / `gmail_google` / `gmail_unknown`) by `_normalize_sender_to_source`, and the only one with a streak-counter side effect (3-strike auth-failure ntfy escalation). New class `findajob.fetchers.adapters.gmail.GmailLinkedInAdapter` with class-attr `source_label = "gmail"` (the *adapter-level* identifier for admin UX and registry-membership invariants); per-row `source` is set inside `fetch()`. The asymmetry between adapter-level and per-row source labels is intentional and unique to Gmail — the Protocol stays uniform across adapters and is **not** generalized to handle dynamic source labels until at least one other adapter needs the same shape (#248 Workday and #249 Gem both use static labels, so YAGNI). `since_days` accepted via constructor (`GmailLinkedInAdapter(since_days=14)`) rather than the Protocol's `fetch(queries)` signature, so the Protocol shape stays uniform; #410.5 orchestrator will pass it through. `is_configured()` returns `gmail_imap.load_config() is not None`. `live_test()` calls `gmail_imap.test_login(config)` and maps **all four** `TestResult` values explicitly: `SUCCESS` → `success`, `AUTH_FAILED` → `auth`, `CONNECTION_ERROR` → `network`, **`INVALID_CONFIG` → `auth`** (config parses but fails IMAP-side validation — same UX class as auth-failed; user must fix at `/config/gmail/`). Without an explicit INVALID_CONFIG mapping the bucket would fall through to a wrong default; mapping it explicitly so a future TestResult value doesn't silently mis-bucket. `live_test()` also routes the not-configured case to `auth` with an actionable error message pointing to `/config/gmail/`. **Hot-zone behavior preserved**: the auth-failure streak counter still increments on each AUTH_FAILED, ntfys exactly once on the 2→3 transition (`if new_streak == 3:` exact equality), and resets to 0 on success. New regression test `test_fetch_does_not_refire_ntfy_after_streak_passes_three` locks in the exact-equality intent — AUTH_FAILED at streak=3 advances to 4 but does NOT re-fire the ntfy, so a future "fix" changing `==` to `>=` fails CI loudly rather than silently spamming the operator every 30 minutes. Helpers `_normalize_sender_to_source`, `parse_jobs_from_email_imap`, `_extract_jobs_from_html`, `notify_send_raw` left at `findajob.fetchers.__init__.py` and imported by the adapter — moving them is out of scope for this PR. Old `fetch_gmail_jobs(since_days=None)` becomes a thin wrapper that constructs the adapter — preserves `triage/orchestrator.py:105` (the only remaining caller; `_gmail_disclosure.html` reference is a doc-link string, not an import) until #410.5 cuts the orchestrator over to `iter_configured_adapters()` exclusively. New `tests/test_gmail_adapter.py` (13 tests: 2 `is_configured`, 6 `fetch` covering the four migrated `fetch_gmail_jobs` integration tests + the new streak=4 no-refire regression + `since_days` constructor passthrough, 5 `live_test` buckets including the explicit INVALID_CONFIG mapping and not-configured fallback). The four migrated tests at `tests/test_gmail_imap.py:436-543` were deleted with a header comment pointing to the new home — they now exercise the adapter directly per AC #8 ("no test loss"). New entry in `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS` + `gmail` line in `config/active_sources.txt.example`.
- **#410.3 feat(fetchers): `LeverAdapter` — migrate `fetch_lever_jobs` to JobSourceAdapter framework.** Third of five sub-PRs implementing the #410 Epic. New class `findajob.fetchers.adapters.lever.LeverAdapter` follows the canonical Protocol shape (`is_configured`/`fetch`/`live_test`); `is_configured()` true when `config/feed_urls.txt` contains at least one `lever.co/...` URL; `fetch()` returns the existing `source="lever_json"` row shape unchanged. Lever's posting API returns a top-level JSON array (not `{"jobs": [...]}` like Ashby/Greenhouse) — `isinstance(data, list)` guard preserved at both `fetch()` (skip slug, log `unexpected_format`) and `live_test()` (return `server` bucket with explicit "unexpected format" message rather than crashing on `len(dict)`). `live_test()` 404 → `auth` (Lever's public posting API has no auth so we treat invalid slugs as the same UX class as RapidAPI 401/403), 429 → `rate_limit` and 5xx → `server` defensively (Lever doesn't document either, but mis-bucketing them as auth failures would render the wrong error card). Old `fetch_lever_jobs(feed_urls_path)` becomes a thin wrapper that constructs the adapter — preserves `triage/orchestrator.py` until #410.5 cuts the orchestrator over to `iter_configured_adapters()` exclusively. Reuses `_parse_feed_slugs` from `findajob.fetchers.adapters._slugs` (introduced in #410.2). Asymmetry preserved with intent: legacy `fetch_lever_jobs` had **no** Timeout retry (unlike Ashby's one-shot retry) — `LeverAdapter.fetch()` does not add one. Different vendors get different politeness budgets, and adding a retry loop the legacy code didn't have is exactly the kind of "while we're here" change that a behavior-preserving migration should refuse. Now-unused `re` import + `_parse_feed_slugs` import dropped from `findajob/fetchers/__init__.py` (both Ashby and Lever wrappers are 6-line constructors). New `tests/test_lever_adapter.py` (17 tests: `is_configured` 3 cases, `fetch` happy path with array response, display-name-from-comment, descriptionPlain→description fallback, 403 skip, **non-list response skip**, no-Timeout-retry assertion, 7 `live_test` buckets including the array-shape `server` bucket and defensive 429+5xx). New entry in `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS` + `lever` line in `config/active_sources.txt.example`. Existing tester stacks running `:v0.22` are unaffected (their `active_sources.txt` does not auto-update from the example).
- **#410.2 feat(fetchers): `AshbyAdapter` — migrate `fetch_ashby_jobs` to JobSourceAdapter framework + extract shared `_parse_feed_slugs` helper.** Second of five sub-PRs implementing the #410 Epic. New class `findajob.fetchers.adapters.ashby.AshbyAdapter` follows the canonical Protocol shape (`is_configured`/`fetch`/`live_test`); `is_configured()` true when `config/feed_urls.txt` contains at least one `ashbyhq.com/...` URL; `fetch()` returns the existing `source="ashby_json"` row shape unchanged (preserves the dict-shaped-`location` normalization, the `descriptionHtml`→`descriptionPlain` fallback, the inline-comment-as-`company` resolution from the helper, and the one-shot Timeout retry from the legacy fetcher); `live_test()` 404 → `auth` (Ashby's public API has no auth so we treat invalid slugs as the same UX class as RapidAPI 401/403), 429 → `rate_limit` and 5xx → `server` defensively (Ashby doesn't document either, but mis-bucketing them as auth failures would lead the form to render the wrong error card). Old `fetch_ashby_jobs(feed_urls_path)` becomes a thin wrapper that constructs the adapter — preserves `triage/orchestrator.py` until #410.5. Shared helper `_parse_feed_slugs` (Ashby + Lever both consume the `# Display Name` URL convention) extracted from `findajob/fetchers/__init__.py` to a new private module `findajob/fetchers/adapters/_slugs.py` matching the `_keys.py` / `_locations.py` underscore-prefix convention; `fetch_lever_jobs` updated to import from the new home, behavior unchanged until #410.3 migrates Lever. New `tests/test_fetchers_slug_helper.py` (7 tests: dedup keeps first occurrence, inline `# Display Name` honored, missing file returns `[]`, non-matching lines ignored, both Ashby and Lever regex patterns work, default titlecase, empty-comment falls back to titlecase). New `tests/test_ashby_adapter.py` (16 tests: `is_configured`, `fetch` happy path with display-name-from-comment, dict-shaped location normalization, plain-text description fallback, 403 skip, Timeout retry, all six `live_test` buckets including the defensive 429/5xx paths). New entry in `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS` + `ashby` line in `config/active_sources.txt.example`.
