Existing tester stacks running `:v0.22` are unaffected (they have their own `active_sources.txt` and don't pick up additions to the example).
- **#410.1 feat(fetchers): `GreenhouseAdapter` — migrate `fetch_greenhouse_jobs` to JobSourceAdapter framework.** First of five sub-PRs implementing the #410 Epic. New class `findajob.fetchers.adapters.greenhouse.GreenhouseAdapter` follows the canonical Protocol shape (`is_configured`/`fetch`/`live_test`); `is_configured()` true when `config/feed_urls.txt` contains at least one `boards.greenhouse.io` / `boards.eu.greenhouse.io` / `job-boards.greenhouse.io` / `job-boards.eu.greenhouse.io` URL; `fetch()` returns the existing `source="greenhouse_json"` row shape unchanged; `live_test()` 404 → `auth` bucket (treats invalid slugs as config failure, same UX card as RapidAPI 401/403). Old `fetch_greenhouse_jobs(feed_urls_path)` becomes a thin wrapper that constructs the adapter — preserves `triage/orchestrator.py:102` until #410.5 cuts the orchestrator over to `iter_configured_adapters()` exclusively. Slug-extraction test coverage migrated from `tests/test_fetchers_greenhouse_slug.py` (deleted) to `tests/test_greenhouse_adapter.py::TestSlugExtraction` (all 7 canonical cases preserved per AC #4: classic + EU + job-boards + job-boards-EU subdomains, bare-slug shapes, dedup across shapes, mixed-file with comments). New entry in `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS` + `greenhouse` line in `config/active_sources.txt.example` so new stacks pick it up by default. Existing tester stacks running `:v0.22` are unaffected (they have their own `active_sources.txt`).

### Added
- **#603 feat(web): `/settings/active-sources/` — operator UI for adapter selection + dashboard banner.** Second occupant of the `/settings/` namespace (after `/settings/reject-reasons/` #490). Mirrors that pattern: `GET /settings/active-sources/` renders a checkbox list of every `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS` entry with a per-row `is_configured()` badge ("✓ Fetchable" / "✗ Not configured" with hover tooltip explaining what's missing); pre-checked from `config/active_sources.txt` if present, from `_DEFAULT_ACTIVE_SOURCES` if absent. `POST /settings/active-sources/` validates submitted names against `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS` (rejects unknowns with the offending name in the error message), writes the selection atomically (tmp + `os.replace`) preserving registry order, returns an HTMX `success` partial. New helper `_write_active_sources(names: list[str], path: Path | None = None) -> None` lives in `findajob.fetchers.adapters.registry` next to the existing `_read_active_sources`. Empty selection → header-only file → `_read_active_sources` falls back to `_DEFAULT_ACTIVE_SOURCES` (intentional: "uncheck everything → revert to default" UX). New dashboard banner at the top of `/board/dashboard` (above the rejections widget) appears iff `active_sources.txt` is absent AND the `active_sources_banner_dismissed` cookie is unset; banner copy includes the count of currently-fetchable default adapters and a "Don't show again" link that POSTs `?dismiss_active_sources_banner=1`, sets a 1-year cookie, and 303-redirects back. Banner suppressed once the file exists (regardless of cookie) — operator's explicit choice trumps the prompt. Tests: 12 in `tests/test_routes_settings_active_sources.py` covering GET render with default + custom state, per-adapter badge rendering, POST happy path + round-trip through `_read_active_sources`, validation rejection with file-untouched assertion, atomic-write spy on `os.replace`, banner show/hide across the three states (file absent + no cookie → show; file present → suppressed; cookie set → suppressed). Routes registered under the existing `_guard` (onboarding-complete) dependency in `findajob.web.routes.__init__`. **No `migration-required`** — additive UI; existing stacks unaffected (file-absent stacks see the banner once and decide; file-present stacks see no UX change). Closes #603.

- **#422 feat(adapters): `JobsApi14BingAdapter` — Bing endpoint as separate adapter.** Sibling of `JobsApi14IndeedAdapter` (#414) and `JobsApi14Adapter` (LinkedIn). Ingests via jobs-api14's `/v2/bing/search` endpoint, returning rows with `source='jobsapi_bing'`. Inline `description` ingestion (no separate `/v2/bing/get` round-trip — same as Indeed). Single-page only initially — Bing's 18 jobs/page already beats LinkedIn's 10; multi-page support deferred (no `JOBS_API14_BING_MAX_PAGES` env var) per AC's design section. Shares the canonical `RAPIDAPI_KEY` (or legacy `JOBS_API14_KEY` fallback per #414) with the LinkedIn + Indeed adapters — same RapidAPI account, same per-account quota; on PRO-tier 20,000 req/month is shared across all three. **Default-off, opt-in only**: `JobsApi14BingAdapter` is added to `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS` (so the #512 Protocol-conformance test and #516 registry-membership invariant see it) but intentionally **omitted from `_DEFAULT_ACTIVE_SOURCES`** — the first adapter to follow this opt-in pattern post-#410.5 (existing adapters' inclusion in the default preserves pre-cutover effective behavior; new adapters require explicit opt-in via `config/active_sources.txt`). Operators enable by adding `jobs-api14-bing` to `config/active_sources.txt`; `config/active_sources.txt.example` ships a commented `# jobs-api14-bing` line documenting the opt-in. **No title-allowlist post-filter initially** — AC #4 calls for an empirical decision after one triage-day measurement of Bing's natural keyword-match quality; deferred to **#601** (cross-ref'd to #417 + #228). Until that measurement decides, all titles flow through; new regression test `test_fetch_passes_all_titles_through_when_no_allowlist` locks in the allow-all contract so a future "while we're here" allowlist add fails CI loudly. Defensive params (query + location + countryCode=us + sortType=date) mirror the conservative posture used for Indeed at #414 PR1; Bing's per-call filter surface (datePosted, employmentTypes, etc.) is unverified at PR time and a fast-follow can expand if operator's first triage day shows we'd benefit. Response-shape assumption mirrors Indeed's payload (`applyUrl`, inline `description`, `company.name`, `location.location`); operator's first triage day will validate against the real API and a fast-follow PR adjusts if Bing's actual shape diverges. New `tests/test_jobs_api14_bing_adapter.py` (13 tests): class attributes, `is_configured` 3 cases, fetch happy path with assumed Bing response shape, drops-no-title-or-url, allow-all-titles regression lock, 429 retry, hasError handling, 2 `live_test` buckets. `docs/getting-started/api-keys.md` adapter table gains a Bing row + an opt-in note (with the deferred-allowlist caveat called out explicitly so operators reading the docs understand the tuning gap). `data/.env.example` shared-key comment updated to mention Bing alongside LinkedIn / Indeed. **No `migration-required`** — opt-in only; existing stacks without `active_sources.txt` get the post-#410.5 default which doesn't include Bing. Closes #422. Empirical-allowlist follow-up tracked separately.

### Fixed
- **#589 fix(web): `file_serve` 404s on speculative briefing.md before prep is flagged.** `folder_view` was extended in #485 with a synthetic-row fallback that surfaces `briefing.md` from `jobs.speculative_briefing_folder` when no prep folder exists yet, but `file_serve` was never given the matching treatment — clicking **View →** on the rendered "Briefing (speculative)" row 404'd because `resolve_folder` returned None and `file_serve` raised immediately. The folder index was reading from one source of truth and the per-file route from another. Extracted `_resolve_folder_with_speculative_fallback(fingerprint, db, root)` in `src/findajob/web/routes/materials.py` and routed both `folder_view` and `file_serve` through it; the helper preserves the path-traversal guard on the stored folder name and returns `None` only when the row truly has no usable folder. Tests in `tests/test_web_routes.py` cover the four shape axes: rendered-HTML happy path, `?raw=1` byte-identity for the Copy MD button, filename-traversal still rejected once the fallback activates, and 404 when the synthetic row's `speculative_briefing_folder` points to a non-existent dir on disk. The lockstep regression discipline pattern from #582 applies here — both routes now share one resolver, so future fallback paths land in both at once.
- **#586 fix(rejection_detector): subject/body fallback when extraction fails to corroborate.** Closes the architectural coupling between extraction and corroboration: `_find_corroborating_handled_job` queries by `extracted_company`, so when the classifier's extraction misfired (returned None or a wrong token like a role substring), the primary corroboration path silently failed too — already-handled rejections leaked through as suggestions in the review queue. New `_find_corroborating_handled_job_fallback` in `scripts/detect_rejections.py` runs after the primary path returns None: scans the email's subject + body excerpt for any `not_selected`/`rejected` `jobs.company` value with word-boundary regex (`\b...\b`) and a 4-character length floor (`_CORROBORATION_MIN_COMPANY_LEN`) to skip "IBM"/"HP"/"Co"-class false positives. The 4-char floor accepts false-negative corroboration on short-named companies (suggestion gets surfaced, operator dismisses) in exchange for zero false-positive corroboration that would suppress real signals. Decoupled from extraction by design — robust to future extraction-shape regressions we haven't anticipated, including the Anthropic-shape "so much" interjection and Zoox-shape role-token leakage that operator's 2026-05-09 first-run backlog hit. Tests: 4 new in `tests/test_detect_rejections_script.py` covering (1) extraction-fails-but-company-in-body → corroborated, (2) short company names skipped (IBM stays in the queue), (3) word-boundary regex avoids `acme` matching `acmestaff`, (4) generic email with no handled company persists as suggestion. All 10 detect_rejections tests + 101 rejection-detector + adjacent tests pass.
- **#585 fix(rejection_detector): `_INTEREST_RE` + `_POSITION_RE` miss three real rejection-email shapes.** Discovered post-#362 first-run backlog scan against operator's actual Gmail on 2026-05-09: 4 of 5 surfaced suggestions had wrong or missing extracted company. Three classifier-extraction defects + one role-extraction defect were the cause (the fourth issue is corroboration-coupling, tracked separately as #586). `_INTEREST_RE` now accepts (a) the "Thanks" subject shorthand alongside "Thank you" via `(?:thanks?\s+you|thanks)`; (b) up to 3 adverb words between "Thank you" and "for" via `(?:\s+\w+){0,3}` so "Thank you **so much** for your interest in COMPANY" stops being silently rejected; (c) ` as `, ` and `, ` for our/the ` in the terminator alternation so lazy `.+?` capture terminates at the company boundary instead of running to end-of-sentence on shapes like "interest in COMPANY as the next step in your career". `_POSITION_RE` adds `for our` alongside `for the position` / `application for` so role extraction works on bodies like "for our Infrastructure Engineer, Lab Manager role" — previously these emitted None for `extracted_role` and forced the matcher into ambiguous when the company had multiple active applications. Four new redacted `.eml` fixtures landed under `tests/fixtures/rejection_emails/` (lever/thanks_subject_role_in_body.eml, greenhouse/so_much_interjection.eml, ashby/as_the_next_step.eml, ashby/for_our_role.eml), each with a paired regression test that asserts BOTH `confidence='high'` AND that the extraction returned a usable, non-leaking value — the older confidence-only tests passed silently while extraction returned junk like `'Cobot as the next step in your career'`. All 24 classifier tests + 97 rejection-detector + adjacent tests pass.

## [0.22.0] — 2026-05-09

### Migration required
- **#362 (Task 1): migration `0003_rejection_suggestions` adds the `rejection_suggestions` table.** Backs the operator-confirmation queue for Gmail-detected company rejection emails (full feature lands across Tasks 2–6 of the rejection-detection epic). `docker compose pull && docker compose up -d` is the entire migration path — `apply_pending` runs 0003 on first boot, advancing `_meta.schema_version` from 2 → 3 and creating the table + 2 indexes (`rejection_suggestions_user_action`, `rejection_suggestions_matched_job`). Verify post-deploy: `sqlite3 state/data/pipeline.db "SELECT value FROM _meta WHERE key='schema_version'"` → `3`; `sqlite3 state/data/pipeline.db ".schema rejection_suggestions"` → table + indexes. Until subsequent tasks land detector/UI code, the table sits empty — the migration is a forward-compatible no-op for existing flows.

### Added
- **#362 (Task 5) feat(web): rejection-review surface + dashboard widget + `handle_not_selected` `changed_by` param.** Fifth of six PR-sized tasks for #362. New router `src/findajob/web/routes/rejections_review.py` exposes the operator's review queue at `GET /board/rejections-review/` (pending suggestions newest-detected first) plus three POST endpoints — `confirm` (calls `handle_not_selected(..., changed_by='gmail_rejection_detector')` on the matched job), `dismiss` (mark `user_action='dismissed'`, leave job stage), and `reattribute` (operator picks a different `jobs.id`, applies to that job, marks `user_action='reassigned'` with `user_chose_job_id` recorded). HTMX-friendly: confirm/dismiss/reattribute return empty 200 on `HX-Request` so the calling card swaps out via `hx-swap="outerHTML"`; non-HTMX POSTs redirect back. Idempotent on double-clicks (re-issued POST against a non-pending row is a no-op). `confirm` 409s when `matched_job_id` is null (operator must reattribute first) or when the matched job's stage isn't in `applied/interview/offer` (mirrors the canonical `_POST_APPLICATION_STAGES` invariant from `board_actions.py:501`). New widget partial `templates/board/_rejections_widget.html` surfaces a pending-count info bar above the dashboard queue when rows exist, nothing when zero — fed by a new `_rejections_pending_count` helper on the `/board/dashboard` route that tolerates pre-#362 stacks via `try/except sqlite3.OperationalError`. New full-page template `templates/rejections_review.html` renders cards with confidence badge, suggested-reason chip, sender-domain ATS hint, body excerpt, extracted company/role, matched-job context, and the three action buttons (Reattribute opens an inline `<details>` form for the job-id paste). Additive `changed_by: str | None = None` keyword param added to `findajob.actions.handle_not_selected`; defaults to `None` so the existing manual flow keeps writing `changed_by='system'`, while the rejection-review confirm/reattribute paths pass `'gmail_rejection_detector'` for traceability per spec §4.5.2. New `config/company_aliases.yaml.example` documents the operator-curated alias config the matcher reads (Task 2 already wired the lookup); `config/company_aliases.yaml` added to the `/config/` editor allowlist and `.gitignore`. Tests: 15 new in `tests/test_routes_rejections_review.py` covering index render with pending-only filter, confirm happy path with audit-tag assertion, the two 409 guards (unmatched and out-of-window stage), 404 on unknown suggestion, double-click idempotency, non-HTMX redirect, dismiss-leaves-job-untouched, reattribute happy path, reattribute-404, widget render+empty-state, and dashboard widget inline render+absence; 2 new in `tests/test_actions.py` covering `changed_by` propagation and the default-`'system'` behavior; 1 new entry in the allowlist parametrized test for `company_aliases.yaml`.
- **#362 (Task 4) feat(scripts): `detect_rejections.py` + cron registration + first-run backlog sweep.** Fourth of six PR-sized tasks for #362. New `scripts/detect_rejections.py` orchestrates the now-merged classifier (Task 2) + IMAP extension (Task 3) into a 30-minute cron entry. Flow: `load_config()` early-exits as no-op when Gmail unconfigured (`pipeline.jsonl` `rejection_scan_skipped`); first run sweeps prior 30 days (default; capped at 60 per spec §4.7) gated by `state.rejection_backlog_scan_complete`; steady-state runs are UID-checkpointed via `state.rejection_last_uid` and advance on every successful run (advisor-flagged guard against re-scanning every cycle); `outcome.result != SUCCESS` paths emit `rejection_scan_failed` with the `TestResult` enum value and exit 0 so transient IMAP hiccups don't fire cron alerts. Spec §4.8 corroborated path lives in the orchestrator: when `match_job` returns `unmatched`, a script-local secondary lookup fuzzy-matches the email's company against `not_selected`/`rejected` jobs at the matcher's same threshold (rapidfuzz token_set_ratio ≥ 80) — hits log `rejection_email_corroborated` and skip the review queue, so already-handled rejections don't generate noise. ntfy throttled to one notification per cycle (§4.6) with backlog-aware messaging; `cta_url` routes to `/board/rejections-review/` (Task 5). New `ops/scheduled-jobs.yaml` entry `detect-rejections` runs `*/30 * * * *` with `${FINDAJOB_DETECT_REJECTIONS_TIMEOUT:-600}` per the #344 env-var override convention. New `tests/test_detect_rejections_script.py` (6 tests) covers the no-op path, first-run backlog sentinel flip with the default-window assertion, the `not_selected` corroborated-event-no-row path, the steady-state UID checkpoint advance, the IMAP-failure surface, and the matched-suggestion DB persistence. Smoke verified end-to-end: script returns 0 with no Gmail config and emits the expected `rejection_scan_skipped` event.
- **#362 (Task 3) feat(gmail): IMAP extension for rejection scanning.** Third of six PR-sized tasks for #362. Strictly additive extension to `findajob.gmail_imap`: new `DEFAULT_REJECTION_ALLOWLIST` covering Greenhouse / Ashby / Lever ATS senders (Workday-style `talent.{company}.com` matched at the rejection_detector layer via suffix); new `GmailConfig.rejection_sender_allowlist` field (default factory); new `GmailState` checkpoint fields `rejection_last_uid` / `rejection_backlog_scan_complete` / `rejection_backlog_window_days`; new `fetch_new_messages_for_rejection_scan(config, state, since_days=None)` parallel to `fetch_new_messages` but reading the rejection allowlist + UID checkpoint. Existing `fetch_new_messages` job-fetch path is **untouched**. Backwards-compatible at the persistence layer: pre-#362 `gmail.json` (no `rejection_sender_allowlist`) and `gmail_state.json` (no rejection-checkpoint keys) load with sensible defaults, no schema bump. Read-only IMAP semantics preserved (BODY.PEEK[]; no STORE/COPY/EXPUNGE/APPEND/MOVE/CREATE/DELETE) — verified by both file-grep `test_gmail_imap_uses_only_read_verbs` and the new runtime-recorder `test_rejection_scan_uses_only_readonly_verbs` in `tests/test_transparency_invariants.py`. New `tests/test_gmail_imap_rejection_scan.py` covers backwards-compat config/state loading, the new function's allowlist source, UID-search shape (`{rejection_last_uid+1}:*`), BODY.PEEK invariant, monotonic UID advance, `since_days` first-run-backlog widening (caller in Task 4), exception-path logout cleanup, and pipeline-event emission (`rejection_email_scanned` per-message + `rejection_scan_completed` per-cycle). 14 new tests; 9 transparency tests still green.
- **#362 (Task 2) feat(rejection_detector): pure-data classifier package.** Second of six PR-sized tasks for #362. New `findajob.rejection_detector/` package implementing the three-layer detection cascade from spec §4.2: (1) known ATS sender + body marker → `confidence='high'`; (2) unknown sender + body marker → `confidence='medium'`; (3) LLM tiebreak deferred. Four modules — `patterns.py` (sender fingerprints + body markers), `parser.py` (RFC 822 + bs4 HTML fallback + whitespace normalization for line-wrapped marker phrases), `classifier.py` (`classify_email(bytes) → RejectionSuggestion | None`), `matcher.py` (alias resolution per §4.2.1, seniority-token gate per §4.2.2). 17 archived `.eml` fixtures under `tests/fixtures/rejection_emails/` covering Greenhouse / Ashby / Lever / Workday / in-house / acks / HTML-only — fixtures must be archived static per spec §3.5 (corpus drift caveat). 39 tests pass: golden-fixture classifier cases, parser shape coverage, matcher disambiguation cases, and the **`_POST_APPLICATION_STAGES` lockstep regression** that fails CI loudly if the matcher's stage filter ever drifts from `findajob.web.routes.board_actions._POST_APPLICATION_STAGES`. Pure-data: no DB I/O, no FastAPI imports — Task 4 wires this into the orchestration script, Task 5 into web routes. New direct dep: `rapidfuzz>=3.0` (token-set ratio for company/role matching; spec assumed it was already in but it wasn't).
- **#362 (Task 1) feat(schema): migration 0003 — `rejection_suggestions` table.** First of six PR-sized tasks implementing #362 (auto-detect company rejection emails via Gmail). The table is the write-once dedup log keyed by `gmail_message_id` for emails the detector classifies as rejections; rows hold the matched `jobs.id` (if matcher succeeded), `confidence` (`high`/`medium`), `suggested_reason` (one of the reject_reason taxonomy entries), and `user_action` (`pending`/`confirmed`/`dismissed`/`reassigned`). Indexes cover the two main query shapes: pending-queue badge count (`user_action`) and per-job suggestion lookup (`matched_job_id`). Routes through the M5 versioned migration runner (#553) — no manual SQL on deploy. Spec: `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-01-362-rejection-detection-design.md` §4.3 (operator-private). Existing `tests/test_background_tasks_schema.py::test_background_tasks_in_schema_version_2` relaxed from a `== 2` head-version pin to `>= 2` floor (background_tasks ships at 2 and remains available at later head versions).

### Changed
- **#561 feat(web): speculative status page surfaces `background_tasks` info (M6 follow-up).** The `/speculative/status/{id}` page (and its HTMX poll fragment) now joins the latest `background_tasks` row for the request and shows: subprocess `started_at` + `pid` while `researching`; subprocess error_message as a fallback when `speculative_requests.error_message` is empty (catches Popen failures from `record_failed` that the workflow-level handler can't see); `finished_at` on the failed branch. New helper `findajob.web.routes.speculative._latest_bg_task` fetches by `(kind='speculative_research', job_id=str(request_id))` ordered by `id DESC` so the regenerate path's newest run wins. Pre-M6 stacks lacking `background_tasks` still render — `bg_task` falls through as `None` and the conditional template blocks skip. Closes the M6 epic body's E1.I4 follow-up. **Out of scope (separately filable):** an operator-mode `/tasks/` page listing all in-flight `background_tasks` rows; prep status currently has no dedicated page (the dashboard row stage is the operator's signal).

- **#559 feat(admin): `stack_health.stuck_prep_count` reads from `background_tasks` (M6 follow-up).** Migrates the operator-mode dashboard's stuck-prep count from the pre-M6 query (`jobs.stage='prep_in_progress' AND stage_updated < cutoff`) to M6's canonical signal (`background_tasks WHERE status='running' AND kind='prep' AND started_at < cutoff`). Same 60min threshold via `KIND_TIMEOUT_MINUTES['prep']` imported from `findajob.background_tasks`. The new source eliminates two failure modes: subprocess crashes that didn't update `stage_updated` are now visible, and stale stages with no recent activity no longer false-positive. Pre-M6 stacks lacking `background_tasks` are tolerated via `try/except sqlite3.OperationalError` → 0 (same shape as the existing `notifications` lookup). Closes the M6 epic body's "Out of M6 scope" follow-up. Test fixture `tests/conftest_admin.py::build_pipeline_db` now routes through `apply_pending` (eliminates fixture-vs-production drift) and accepts a `bg_tasks` parameter for inserting `background_tasks` rows. The `test_stuck_prep_counts_only_over_60min` test exercises the new query against an `apply_pending`-built fixture with backdated `background_tasks` rows covering the four shape axes (running/finished, prep/interview_prep, fresh/stuck).

- **#568 ci: bump GitHub Actions to Node.js 24-compatible versions ahead of deprecation.** GitHub flagged Node 20 as deprecated on every workflow run since the v0.21.0 cohort wave; runner default switches to Node 24 on **2026-06-02** and Node 20 is removed entirely on **2026-09-16**. Bumped four actions to their first Node-24-default major releases (verified via upstream release notes): `actions/checkout@v4`→`@v5`, `docker/setup-buildx-action@v3`→`@v4`, `docker/login-action@v3`→`@v4`, `docker/build-push-action@v6`→`@v7`. Eleven `uses:` lines updated across `build-image.yml`, `create-release.yml`, `ci.yml`, `pii-scan.yml`. `actions/setup-python@v5` was already Node-24-compatible (absent from the deprecation list) — unchanged. Verification: CI on the PR confirmed the Node 20 deprecation annotation no longer appears on workflow runs and the build/test/release flows still pass.

### Fixed
- **fix(smoke): update `scripts/test_container_integration.sh` doc-slug list to match the post-cleanup `/docs/` routes.** The May-8 docs-cleanup wave (#499–#503) renamed `docs/setup/*` → `docs/getting-started/*` and updated `findajob.web.routes.docs._PAGES` accordingly, but the pre-tag smoke script's slug-reachability loop still tested `setup` and `setup/install-docker`. The script silently exited with the failed-route stack-down whenever it ran post-#500. Caught during the v0.22 pre-tag smoke; fix is mechanical (replace the two stale slugs with `getting-started` and `getting-started/install-docker`). The smoke is the release gate, so this fix had to ride with the release commit rather than wait for a follow-up.
- **#560 fix(schema): document the `company_signal` + `feedback_version` 0001 drift as intentional.** Investigation surfaced both columns are dead — `company_signal` was deprecated in commit `bd59e3c` with 0 rows populated in production; `feedback_version` retains 196/~15k rows of historical data but no current code path references either name (`git grep` across `src/`, `scripts/`, `tests/` returns empty). Per the issue body's decision tree (dead → don't add to 0001 → preserve existing-stack data → document), the fix is comment-only: a §"Intentionally-absent columns" block was added to `migrations/0001_initial.sql` headers explaining why the production drift is deliberate, and two tripwire tests in `test_db_migrate.py` lock the property — one asserts the columns stay absent from 0001's DDL, the other asserts no `src/`/`scripts/` Python file references either name. If a future feature wants to revive either column, the right move is a new numbered migration with `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS`-style guarding; never edit 0001. Note: 0001 has now shipped fresh on `findajob-test` (the v0.21.0 cohort wave applied it from scratch on that stack), so the file's append-only rule applies — comment-only edits are safe but DDL edits are not.

### Refactor
- **#558 refactor(analyze_feedback): extract `scripts/analyze_feedback.py` to `findajob.analyze_feedback` module (M3+).** Same shape as #557 (find_contacts extraction). 459 LOC of feedback-loop analysis (rejection breakdown, false-positive analysis, title keyword signals, n-gram prefilter candidates, format_report, CLI main) move to `src/findajob/analyze_feedback.py`. `scripts/analyze_feedback.py` shrinks to a 17-LOC entry-point shim. Subprocess invocation from `findajob.notifications.feedback_review` (`--json` mode) unchanged. Module-load `load_reject_reasons()` (originally line 240 of the script — populated `_TITLE_SIGNAL_REASONS` at module scope) moved into `_prefilter_candidates()` so importing the module is side-effect-free. **Removes the dynamic-import hack flagged in M3's cleanup PR (#544):** `findajob.notifications.scoreboard` previously did `sys.path.insert(0, f"{BASE}/scripts") + from analyze_feedback import analyze` — now does a direct top-level `from findajob.analyze_feedback import analyze as feedback_analyze`. Test coverage added: `test_analyze_feedback_import_safety.py` (5 tests: load_reject_reasons not called at import, load_env not called at import, public surface exposed, scoreboard imports from canonical location) and `test_analyze_feedback.py` (4 tests: empty-feedback early-return, populated-DB documented-shape, format_report renders, _prefilter_candidates filters by title-signal-reasons). Comment refs in `findajob.config_loader.load_reject_reasons` docstring and `findajob.web.routes.stats` updated to point at the new module path.

- **#557 refactor(find_contacts): extract `scripts/find_contacts.py` to `findajob.find_contacts` module (M3+).** Same shape as the four script→package extractions M3 already shipped (#539 / #541 / #542 / #543). Logic moved to `src/findajob/find_contacts.py` (single module — file is 245 LOC, well under the 300 LOC soft cap, no need to split further). `scripts/find_contacts.py` shrinks to a 10-LOC entry-point shim that imports `main` from the package; subprocess invocation from `findajob.prep.orchestrator` is unchanged. Module-load `load_env()` (line 47 of the original) moved into `main()`, locking the import-safety property characterized by the new `tests/test_find_contacts_import_safety.py` (4 tests: load_env not called at import, `main`/logic-helpers exposed, blank-string guard preserved). Existing `tests/test_find_contacts.py` (#184 / #164 regressions) and `tests/test_find_contacts_cost_logging.py` (Phase 2 cost-log tests) updated to import from the new path. Type annotations added on the public surface — strict mypy is satisfied for the relocated module under M7's gate. First M3+ extraction PR.

- **#556 refactor(prep_naming): consolidate `abbrev_title()` duplication (M3+).** First M3+ punch-list item from the closed M3 epic (#537). `abbrev_title()` was duplicated between `findajob.prep.orchestrator` (typed) and `scripts/rename_folders.py` (untyped); both copies kept in sync by code review rather than code structure. Consolidated to `findajob.prep_naming` (the natural home — same domain as `safe_filename_part`, both build folder-safe filename components). Both call sites import from there. `tests/test_prep_import_safety.py::test_orchestrator_exposes_main_and_abbrev_title` renamed to `test_orchestrator_exposes_main` (orchestrator's deliberate public symbol is `main`; `abbrev_title` is now an import); `test_abbrev_title_behavior` updated to import from the canonical location, mirroring the no-re-export-theater discipline established by the M3 cleanup PR (#544).

## [0.21.0] — 2026-05-08

Minor bump shipping the structural-refactor close-out arc and governance scaffolding for open-source launch readiness. The five-milestone refactor track from `5-refactor-roadmap.md` is now complete: M1 (docs cleanup, #499–#508 series), M3 (script→package extractions for triage, notify, prep, interview — #537 series), M4 (centralized `findajob.db.connect` helper + `utils.py` split — #546 / #548 / #550), M5 (versioned migration runner — #552), M6 (`background_tasks` observability table replacing filesystem sentinels — #554), M7 (strict mypy gate for `findajob.*` — #563). Plus standard OSS scaffolding: `CONTRIBUTING.md` (#505), `SECURITY.md` (#506), `.github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/` + `PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md` (#507).

**Migration required** — M5 (#552) and M6 (#554) introduce a versioned migration runner that ships schema changes through `_meta.schema_version`. See the Migration block below for the verification commands. Operator's stack and `findajob-test` track `:latest`; tester stacks (alice, papa, dave, judy, tango) currently on `:v0.20` bump to `:v0.21` in this cohort wave.

### Migration required

- **`docker compose pull && docker compose up -d` is the entire migration path.** First boot under the new image runs `apply_pending` from `init_db.py`. On stacks coming from `:v0.20` (every active stack), the runner's heuristic detects equilibrium shape and stamps `_meta.schema_version=1` with **zero DDL**, then runs `0002_background_tasks.sql` to create the `background_tasks` table + 2 indexes (`schema_version` becomes 2). On fresh installs, `0001_initial.sql` runs from scratch followed by `0002`.
- **Verify post-deploy** on each stack:
  ```bash
  sqlite3 state/data/pipeline.db "SELECT value FROM _meta WHERE key='schema_version'"   # → 2
  sqlite3 state/data/pipeline.db ".schema background_tasks"                              # → table + indexes
  ```
- **Optional cleanup:** the `.interview_prep_in_progress` filesystem sentinels from the pre-M6 design are no longer written or read; existing ones sit harmlessly. To reclaim them: `find state/companies -name '.interview_prep_in_progress' -delete`.
- **Auth gate verification** post-recompose remains required per the standing rule (CLAUDE.md "Auth Gate Must Be Verified Post-Deploy"): `docker exec <stack>-scheduler-1 python -m findajob.web.verify_auth` should exit 0 on every stack with auth configured.

### Removed
- **#508 chore(scripts): deleted 5 dead `migrate_*.py` files.** Each represented a one-shot migration that already landed on every active stack and was unreferenced anywhere else in the codebase (verified via `git grep`). Deleted: `scripts/migrate_add_loose_fingerprint.py`, `scripts/migrate_add_user_notes.py`, `scripts/migrate_add_waitlisted.py`, `scripts/migrate_ashby_lever_company_names.py`, `scripts/migrate_cost_log_columns.py`. **No migration required** — each migration already ran. The future versioned migration runner (#9) will replace the ad-hoc pattern these scripts represented.

### Changed
- **#530 docs(pii): evicted residual real-name leaks from tracked content.** Two surfaces touched: a test-fixture string in `tests/test_utils.py::TestCleanProfileField` (replaced with a neutral placeholder name), and one historical CHANGELOG entry (the `#314` PII-scan workflow note) that originally named a specific person and a literal regex pattern containing that person's surname (rewritten to describe the failure mode generically while preserving what shipped). Public-handle aliases used elsewhere in the repo (operator-chosen anonymized labels for testers and stacks) stay — those aren't personal info. Wide grep for first/last names across `git ls-files` returns empty after the change.

### Added
- **#507 feat(governance): added `.github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/` + `PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md`.** Encodes the project's filing discipline so contributors don't have to read CLAUDE.md to comply. New files: `.github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/bug.yml` (structured form: summary, repro steps, expected vs actual, image tag/version, log slice, environment context — auto-applies the `bug` label and points security-relevant reports at `SECURITY.md`); `.github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/feature.yml` (summary, motivation, proposed acceptance criteria, alternatives — auto-applies `enhancement`); `.github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/config.yml` (keeps blank-issue creation enabled for the operator's quick-file workflow + adds Discussions and Security-advisory contact links); `.github/PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md` (Conventional Commits type checkbox, **migration-required** self-check, tests checkbox, AC checklist, linked-issue reference). The discipline mirrors what CONTRIBUTING.md describes — the templates make it the path of least resistance.

- **#506 feat(governance): added `SECURITY.md` at repo root.** Standard OSS scaffolding for vulnerability disclosure. Defines: supported versions (`:latest` and the current `:vMAJOR.MINOR` moving alias receive security patches; immutable patch tags do not), the private disclosure path (GitHub's "Report a vulnerability" private advisory thread — no email address that would re-introduce PII), response timeline (7-day acknowledgement, 14-day triage, 30-day fix target for high-severity, 90-day default disclosure window), in-scope surfaces (basic-auth gate, state write surface, LLM transport, per-stack key isolation invariant, pre-commit PII protection, onboarding flow), and out-of-scope residual risks (LLM prompt injection from JD content; operator deployment topology; third-party API key abuse; routine dependency CVEs covered by Dependabot). README's "Stay in touch / contribute" section now links forward.

- **#505 feat(governance): added `CONTRIBUTING.md` at repo root.** Forkers previously had to reverse-engineer the pre-commit hook setup, the test-suite invocation, and the issue/PR conventions. Now there's a single starting point. Covers: bug reports + feature requests, dev environment setup (`uv sync` + `uv run pytest` + ruff invocation), pre-commit hook install (with the operator-private vs tester-fork distinction), Conventional Commits prefixes, the PR-vs-commit-to-main flow table from CLAUDE.md, the `migration-required` label criteria, the pre-PR checklist, the architectural invariants (SQLite-as-SoT, Web-as-write-surface, LLM-via-openrouter.complete, JobSourceAdapter Protocol, hard-rejects-are-code, paths-via-findajob.paths), code style + patterns (what to follow, what to retreat from on every pass-through), file-size soft caps, tests-required-when, when-to-split-a-refactor, dependency-add criteria, and pointers to `docs/maintainers/`. README's "Stay in touch / contribute" section now links forward to `CONTRIBUTING.md`. Source: lifted from CLAUDE.md §"Implementation Guardrails" closing note ("the full PR + maintainer checklists … will be promoted into CONTRIBUTING.md as part of Open-Source Launch Readiness"). The abridged form stays in CLAUDE.md as durable Claude-facing guidance.
