### Added
- **#515 admin/* SQLite URI invariants test.** AST-based static-analysis sweep over `src/findajob/admin/*.py` and `src/findajob/web/routes/admin*.py`. Every `sqlite3.connect(...)` call must pass a `file:` URI containing both `mode=ro` and `immutable=1` plus `uri=True` in kwargs — locks the cross-stack-reader contract. Resolves indirection (e.g., `uri = f"file:..."` then `sqlite3.connect(uri, uri=True)`) by tracing local string assignments within the enclosing function. Current call site at `findajob.admin.stack_health` is compliant; any future admin reader that drifts from the pattern fails the test with `file:line:reason`. Memory: `feedback_immutable_for_cross_stack_sqlite` (foreign-uid readers break under default `mode=ro` because the producer's WAL/shm sidecar is unreadable).
- **#510 audit_log coverage in board_actions matrix (gap-fill batch 1).** `TestReject` and `TestNotSelected` previously verified HTTP, stage, feedback_log, and folder side-effects but did not assert on `audit_log` rows even though `handle_rejection`/`handle_not_selected` write two entries each (`stage` + `reject_reason`). Adds three tests covering both transitions, the idempotent-skip no-op, and tightens `TestApplySyntheticBranch.test_real_apply_does_not_use_outreach_button` (renamed to `test_real_apply_writes_user_changed_by`) from a weak `!=` to a positive `== 'user'` assertion per the CLAUDE.md Synthetic Jobs Convention contract.
- **#513 #514 schema baseline regression tests.** Two paired tests lock the schema contract before the M3+ structural refactor work: `tests/test_schema_baseline_fresh.py` asserts that a fresh `init_db.py` against an empty tmpdir matches a committed JSON snapshot at `tests/fixtures/schema_baseline_fresh.json`; `tests/test_schema_baseline_legacy.py` asserts that a v0.10.0-shape fixture run through the production deployment arc (`init_db.py` + `migrate_schema()`) ends up structurally identical to the fresh baseline. The snapshot captures `sqlite_master.sql` text per object (whitespace + comment normalized) alongside structured PRAGMA output, so `CHECK` constraints and partial-index `WHERE` clauses are part of the contract — not just columns and FKs. To regenerate the snapshot when a schema change is intentional: `UPDATE_SCHEMA_SNAPSHOT=1 uv run pytest tests/test_schema_baseline_fresh.py`. Drift now fails the test and forces an explicit migration decision in the same PR.

### Added
- **#511 test(board_actions): notes endpoint concurrency + N-POST audit invariant.** Locks two contracts the existing `TestNotes` suite did not cover: five sequential POSTs to `/board/jobs/{fp}/notes` produce zero `audit_log` rows total (using a new `_count_total_audit_rows` helper that runs raw `COUNT(*)` rather than the JOIN-based fetch which would silently miss orphan writes), and two threads POSTing different bodies concurrently both return 200 with the row in a valid final state and no SQLite-locking error surfaced. Mutation-verified: injecting an `INSERT INTO audit_log` into the notes handler causes both new tests to fail. Locks the server contract the JS 800ms debounce relies on so M3+ refactors that add work in the handler can't quietly regress audit silence or concurrency safety.

- **#512 #516 test(adapters): bidirectional Protocol/registry invariants.** Two directions of the `JobSourceAdapter` contract, bundled because they share fixture infrastructure. Registry-to-Protocol: parametrized over `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS`, asserts each entry instantiates without args, satisfies the `runtime_checkable` Protocol, populates required class attrs, and that `name` values are unique (preventing silent shadowing via `active_sources.txt`). Discovery-to-registry: walks `findajob.fetchers.adapters` via `pkgutil.iter_modules` + structural attr/method matching, asserting every adapter-shaped class is in `REGISTERED_ADAPTERS` — catches "wrote it, forgot to register". Discovery uses structural matching rather than `__subclasses__()` because adapters are duck-typed against the Protocol, not subclassed. Mutation-verified against an orphan adapter and a Protocol-violating mutation.

- **#552 refactor(db): versioned migration runner; closes M5.** Replaces three scattered migration entry points (inline ALTERs in `init_db.py`, `migrate_schema()` called from FastAPI startup, ad-hoc one-shot scripts) with a single centralized runner: `findajob.db.migrate.apply_pending(conn)`, called from `init_db.py` at every container start. Schema state is tracked in a new `_meta` table; migration files ship inside the package at `src/findajob/migrations/0001_initial.sql`. The runner uses a heuristic backfill on stacks lacking `_meta` — equilibrium-shape detection stamps `schema_version=1` with zero DDL (the common case for every active stack on `:v0.20`), legacy v0.10 drift triggers a procedural bridge before stamping. Each migration runs in its own transaction with the version-row update committed atomically. `scripts/init_db.py` shrank from ~200 LOC to ~30 LOC; `migrate_schema()` in `session_store.py` deleted; `findajob.db` became a package (re-exporting `connect()` so all 32 inbound import sites stay unchanged); 8 test fixtures rebuilt against `apply_pending` to eliminate fixture-vs-production drift. **Migration required** — container restart runs `apply_pending`; verify post-deploy with `sqlite3 pipeline.db "SELECT value FROM _meta WHERE key='schema_version'"` returns 1.

- **#554 refactor(observability): background_tasks table; closes M6.** Replaces filesystem sentinels (`.interview_prep_in_progress`) and stage-time watchdog heuristics with a `background_tasks` table that subprocesses write to directly. New `migrations/0002_background_tasks.sql` defines `(id, job_id, kind, started_at, finished_at, status, error_message, pid)` plus indexes. New `findajob.background_tasks` helper module exposes `record_start` / `record_succeeded` / `record_failed` / `find_stuck` / `find_active_for_subject` plus a `writeback_subprocess` context manager and per-kind timeouts (prep 60min, interview_prep 30min, speculative_research 10min). Four launcher Popen sites (prep, interview_prep, two speculative routes refactored into one) insert a `running` row before spawn, pass `FINDAJOB_BG_TASK_ID` via env, and backfill `pid`. Three orchestrators wrap their main work in `writeback_subprocess`. `scripts/watchdog.py` rewritten as three reaper functions tailing the table; stage reset still routes through `findajob.actions.reset_prep_to_scored`. The interview-prep filesystem sentinel module and its tests are deleted. Surfaced and fixed schema drift in 0001 (the `jobs.stage` CHECK omitted `'not_selected'`); the heuristic backfill gained a table-rebuild dance for legacy stacks since SQLite forbids `ALTER CHECK`. Also the first end-to-end exercise of M5's runner handling a real second migration. **Migration required** — container restart runs `apply_pending`; verify post-deploy with `sqlite3 pipeline.db "SELECT value FROM _meta WHERE key='schema_version'"` returns 2 and the `background_tasks` table exists.

### Changed
- **#546 refactor(db): introduce findajob.db.connect helper.** First child of M4 (#545). Adds a centralized `findajob.db.connect()` helper that replaces three subtly-different `sqlite3.connect(...)` patterns scattered across 32 call sites. Signature exposes four explicit axes covering every pattern in the wild: plain write, cross-stack read (URI form with `mode=ro&immutable=1` + `uri=True`), FastAPI per-request (`check_same_thread=False`), and same-stack read-only. The `cross_stack=True` arg requires `ro=True` — codifies the operator-dashboard read-only invariant as a `ValueError` instead of a doc note. Deliberately does not default `row_factory`, run `PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL`, or wrap a context manager — preserves identical SQL behavior at every site so the M4 sweep is a pure replacement. Pure additive PR; the 32 call-site sweep lands in #548. Mutation-verified: tests catch dropping `immutable=1` and dropping the `ValueError` guard.

- **#548 refactor(db): sweep 32 sqlite3.connect call sites to findajob.db.connect.** Mechanical follow-on to #547. All 32 `sqlite3.connect(...)` sites in `src/findajob/` and `scripts/` now route through the helper, plus `tests/conftest_admin.py`. Five sites pass `timeout=5.0` explicitly to preserve exact pre-helper behavior (Python's default is 5.0; the helper defaults to 30). The single cross-stack site (`admin/stack_health.py`) adopts `cross_stack=True + ro=True`, putting the operator-dashboard read-only invariant under runtime enforcement. Four files dropped now-unused `import sqlite3`. Test-shape migration: deleted `test_admin_sqlite_uri_invariants.py` (its AST-walk has no subjects post-sweep) and replaced it with `test_db_helper_invariants.py` carrying two complementary checks — a global ban on `sqlite3.connect` outside the helper, and an admin-specific assertion that every admin connect passes `cross_stack=True + ro=True`. Three test fixtures that build an isolated findajob package via `PYTHONPATH` now write the real `db.py` into their scratch BASE so behavior matches production.

- **#550 refactor(utils): split utils.py into 5 domain modules; delete utils.py.** Final child of M4. Mechanically partitions `utils.py` (593 LOC, 18 unrelated functions) across five new domain modules — `findajob.audit` (`log_event`, `write_audit`, `LOG_PATH`), `findajob.profile` (candidate-name + voice-sample readers), `findajob.prep_naming` (filename builders), `findajob.classification` (aggregator/synthetic/JD-usability predicates plus `JD_MAX_CHARS` and `strip_jd_boilerplate`), `findajob.llm_parsing` (`extract_json_payload` + `validate_llm_json`) — plus two outlier placements (`quarantine_stale_prep_folders` → `findajob.prep.quarantine`, `load_env` → `findajob.paths`). The two outliers are what enable `utils.py` to be deleted entirely instead of left as a stub; folder maintenance is prep-domain, env-file reading lives next to BASE/config-path resolution. No backwards-compat shim per CLAUDE.md no-backwards-compat-hacks rule. 38 inbound import sites rewritten across `src/`, `scripts/`, and `tests/`. Net M4 effect: a typed single-entry-point DB helper enforcing the cross-stack invariant, 19 utility functions placed by domain instead of in a junk drawer, and `utils.py` gone.

- **#563 refactor(typing): strict mypy gate for findajob.*; closes M7.** Drops `ignore_missing_imports` and the broad `disable_error_code = ["import-untyped"]` for the `findajob.*` namespace; `scripts.*` stays on the lenient default per M7's explicit deferral of entry-point shims. Strictness flags (`warn_unused_ignores`, `warn_redundant_casts`, `no_implicit_optional`, `strict_equality`) move to global `[tool.mypy]` since mypy only allows per-module overrides for import-resolution flags. Dev deps add `types-requests`, `types-PyYAML`, `types-Markdown`, `types-jsonschema`; two third-party imports without upstream stubs (`docx`, `analyze_feedback`) are scoped via per-module overrides rather than `# type: ignore` at import sites. Two real type errors in `findajob.fetchers.__init__` surfaced and were fixed (heterogeneous dict inferred as `dict[str, object]` failed `arg-type`); two now-redundant `# type: ignore[operator]` comments were removed. The seventh and final structural milestone in `5-refactor-roadmap.md` — all roadmap milestones are now closed; remaining cleanup is a defined punch-list, not open-ended refactor scope.

### Refactor
- **#537 refactor(triage): extract scripts/triage.py to findajob.triage package.** First M3 extraction PR. Moves 653 LOC from `scripts/triage.py` into a `findajob.triage` package (`orchestrator`, `contacts`, `null_score_retry`); the script shrinks to a 36-LOC shim. Import-only — preserves cross-script duplication of `notify()` per the M3 epic discipline. The single architectural property created is that `findajob.triage.*` is safe to import without I/O: the SIGTERM handler install, the `pipeline.db` open for `_FEEDBACK_BLOCK`, the `config/roles/*.md` reads for `SCORER_MODEL`, and the `load_env()` parse all moved from module top-level into `main()` (or the entrypoint shim, for the SIGTERM install). New `tests/test_triage_import_safety.py` characterization-tests this property. Three downstream tests dropped their `importlib.util` + `sys.path` workarounds in favor of plain imports.

- **#537 refactor(notify): extract scripts/notify.py to findajob.notifications package.** Second M3 extraction. `scripts/notify.py` shrinks 984 → 22 LOC; the package decomposes into `cli.py` (dispatch), `ntfy.py` (shared infra), and 8 per-command modules (daily_stats, apply_reminder, feedback_review, health_check, issues_ping, ci_check, scoreboard, send_raw). Every module fits under the 300 LOC soft cap. Module-load side-effect hardening: the original ran `_env = load_env()` at import to seed `NTFY_TOPIC`/`NTFY_URL`/`WEB_BASE_URL` globals; after this PR `_runtime()` is a `functools.cache`-d accessor that loads env on first call, never at import. New `tests/test_notify_import_safety.py` locks the invariant via a `load_env` spy. Cross-script `notify()` duplication preserved (consolidated in #544); `analyze_feedback` dynamic-import hack preserved (target is itself an M3+ extraction candidate). Multiple downstream tests simplified after the import-safety hardening.

- **#537 refactor(prep): extract scripts/prep_application.py to findajob.prep package.** Third M3 extraction. `scripts/prep_application.py` shrinks 682 → 45 LOC. Package layout: `orchestrator` (548), `docx_postprocess`, `role_runner`, `__init__`. The proposed `validation.py` from #538's layout was dropped — extracting the MIN_BYTES + briefing-recommendation block from inside `main()` would be internal restructuring that violates M3's import-only discipline. `load_env()` moved from module top-level into `main()`; new `tests/test_prep_import_safety.py` locks the property. Surfaced a subtle reimport-vs-closure pitfall: the import-safety test reimports only `orchestrator` (which had the original module-load `load_env`) — reimporting `role_runner` would invalidate `from findajob.prep.role_runner import run_role` references taken at collection by other test files, causing later `patch(...)` to silently miss; documented in the test's docstring.

- **#537 refactor(interview): extract scripts/interview_prep.py to findajob.interview package.** Final M3 extraction (4/4). `scripts/interview_prep.py` shrinks 401 → 32 LOC. Three modules — `orchestrator` (288, the first orchestrator under the 300 LOC soft cap), `role_runner` (67), `sentinel` (50). `load_env()` moved into `main()`; new `tests/test_interview_import_safety.py` locks the property. Adds a drift guard for the `run_role()` duplication still present after this PR: compares `findajob.interview.role_runner.run_role.__code__.co_code` against the prep copy and asserts `inspect.signature` equality. Bytecode comparison ignores docstrings/whitespace but catches actual logic drift; pairs with the signature check to catch parameter renames. Drift guard is removed in #544 once the duplication is consolidated.

- **#537 refactor(m3-cleanup): consolidate run_role + notify duplications.** Cleanup PR sequencing the four import-only extractions (#539, #541, #542, #543) by collapsing the duplications they preserved. `run_role()` consolidated 2 → 1 (canonical at `findajob.llm.role_runner`); both per-package copies deleted, prep + interview orchestrators import from the canonical location, and #543's bytecode-equivalence guard is removed since there's only one copy now. `notify()` lightweight ntfy wrapper consolidated 3 → 1 as `quick_notify()` in `findajob.notifications.ntfy` (named distinctly from rich `send()` to preserve no-DB-persistence semantics — background scripts already have their structured audit trail in `pipeline.jsonl` via `log_event`). Dual-source topic lookup (`config/ntfy_topic.txt` first, `data/.env`'s `NTFY_TOPIC` fallback) preserved verbatim. New `tests/test_llm_role_runner.py` locks four invariants: `run_role` signature, both orchestrators import from the canonical location (`is`-equality), the deleted per-package modules raise `ModuleNotFoundError`, and no orchestrator defines a local `notify`. Test-author note in the file's docstring documents why a reimport-based `load_env` spy is deliberately omitted (it would invalidate the suite-wide `run_role` references). Closes M3.

### Removed
- **#499 docs(cleanup): delete onboarding-prework-checklist.md + docs/handoff/.** Phase B of M1 docs cleanup under Epic #377 (Open-Source Launch Readiness). Pure deletions covering retired features and one-off session state. `docs/onboarding-prework-checklist.md` described the retired paste-back onboarding flow (run interview in another LLM, paste emission into `/onboarding/`); the in-app interview has been the single supported path since 2026-05-02. `docs/handoff/2026-05-01-jared-pickup.md` (and the now-empty `docs/handoff/` directory) was a Jared session-handoff note whose Decision-19 references already live in `docs/roadmap.md`. `docs/refactor_recommendations.md` was already removed in S2 close-out and verified absent at PR time. Greps for the deleted slugs across tracked files return zero cross-references; carry-forward punch-list issues (#495, #496, #497, #498) remain open for independent handling.

## [0.20.3] — 2026-05-07

Hotfix on top of v0.20.2 for the #490 settings/reject-reasons editor. Reported by alice within 30 min of the v0.20.2 cohort deploy: clicking "Add reason" did nothing, and the page intro paragraph was developer jargon. Both fixed.

### Fixed
- **#490 Add Reason button broken on `/settings/reject-reasons/`.** Root cause: `{{ rows | tojson }}` was inlined inside `x-data="{ rows: [...], addRow: ... }"`. The JSON contains unescaped `"` characters which close the double-quoted x-data HTML attribute at the first `"text"`. The browser never received Alpine's `addRow` / `removeRow` function definitions, so the `@click` handler was undefined and clicks no-op'd. Standard Jinja+Alpine pitfall. Fix: move the JSON seed into a `<script id="initial-rows" type="application/json">` block and have `x-data` read it via `JSON.parse(document.getElementById('initial-rows').textContent)`. Pinned by new `test_initial_rows_in_script_block_not_inline_x_data`. The TestClient suite cannot exercise Alpine runtime behavior — this regression test asserts on the rendered HTML structure (script block present, `x-data` contains no inline `[{`) so the broken-form recurrence is caught at PR time.

### Changed
- **#490 `/settings/reject-reasons/` page copy rewritten in plain language.** Pre-v0.20.3 intro paragraph used developer jargon ("taxonomy", "scorer", "prefilter candidates", "no recompose required") that meant nothing to non-technical users. Replaced with concrete, action-oriented language: "When you reject a job on your board, you pick a reason from a list. This is that list — add, rename, or remove reasons so the choices match how *you* think about why a job isn't a fit." Title-signal explanation similarly rewritten.

### Migration required

None. Template-only fix on a per-stack-gitignored config editor; no schema, env, compose, or data-shape changes.

## [0.20.2] — 2026-05-07

Patch release shipping the `/settings/reject-reasons/` editor (#490) — beta tester alice's request: tune the reject-reason taxonomy without re-running onboarding. First occupant of the new `/settings/` URL namespace (domain-aware config editors, distinguished from `/config/`'s raw text editor). Bundled along the way: a latent caching bug in `config_loader.load_reject_reasons` + import-time capture in `web/filters/registry.py` that would have made the editor's "no recompose required" promise false. No migration required — `config/reject_reasons.yaml` is already per-stack/gitignored and existing stacks pick up the new editor on `docker compose pull && up -d`.

### Added
- **#490 `/settings/reject-reasons/` editor for `config/reject_reasons.yaml`.** Domain-aware config editor with rich UX: editable rows, per-row `title-signal` checkbox, add/remove via Alpine, HTMX partial-swap save. Lets users tune their rejection taxonomy at any time without re-running the onboarding interview. Server-side validation rejects empty saves, comma-in-reason (URL-filter contract), duplicates, and `title_signal_reasons` not in `reasons`; on validation failure the file is unchanged and an inline error renders. First occupant of `/settings/` — distinguished from `/config/` (raw text editor for allowlisted files); `/settings/` is the home for per-page rich editors. Future similar editors (e.g., for `prefilter_rules.yaml`) live here.

### Changed
- **#490 `findajob.config_loader.load_reject_reasons` no longer caches its result.** File edits are picked up on the next call (small YAML, parse-per-call cost is microseconds). Required so `/settings/reject-reasons/` saves take effect on the next request without a container restart. The module-level `_reject_reasons_cache` is gone; `_reset_cache()` no longer touches it; `test_caches_result` is replaced by `test_no_cache_picks_up_file_changes`. No external behavior change — the dropdown and filter chips already re-resolve per render.
- **#490 `findajob.web.filters.spec.ColumnSpec.enum_values` now accepts `tuple[str, ...] | Callable[[], tuple[str, ...]] | None`.** New `resolved_enum_values` property invokes the callable per access. Eager comma-validation in `__post_init__` is skipped for the callable form (deferred to resolution time). `web/filters/registry.py` switches the reject-reason chip column from a module-level capture to a callable so chip values refresh per request alongside the board's reject-reason dropdown. Two consumer call sites switched to `resolved_enum_values`: `web/filters/url.py:65` and `web/templates/_table_header.html:119`.

### Migration required

None. No schema, config, crontab, mount, or compose changes. `config/reject_reasons.yaml` was already gitignored and per-stack; existing stacks pick up the editor on `docker compose pull` + `docker compose up -d` without any operator action.

## [0.20.1] — 2026-05-07

Patch release on top of v0.20.0 with two web-layer hotfixes: dashboard 5xx under concurrent load (#486) — a SQLite cross-thread bug surfaced post-OpenRouter-migration deploy by HTMX polling on the operator's stack — and a new post-deploy auth-gate verifier + hard rule (#487), triggered by an internet-exposed-without-auth incident on a sibling stack the same day. Also the previously-staged #485 (speculative ingest UX bundle) and #462 (`company_discoverer` cost-threshold ntfy verification) ride along. No migration required; rolls automatically to all stacks pinned to moving aliases.

### Fixed
- **#486 SQLite cross-thread error on dashboard under concurrent load.** Pre-fix, `/board/dashboard` returned HTTP 500 ~85% of the time on the operator's stack running v0.20.0 under any concurrent request load (HTMX polling, multiple browser tabs). Reproduced from inside the container with valid auth: sequential 10/10 → 200; concurrent 17/20 → 500, 3/20 → 200. Root cause: `sqlite3.ProgrammingError: SQLite objects created in a thread can only be used in that same thread.` at `src/findajob/web/app.py:110`. Mechanism: `findajob.web.auth.BasicAuthMiddleware` is a `BaseHTTPMiddleware` subclass; Starlette wraps the inner app in a separate anyio task, which can dispatch `Depends(get_db)` resolution and the route handler to different threadpool workers. The connection was created in thread A and used in thread B, tripping SQLite's default thread-check. Sequential bursts hid the bug because anyio reused a single worker. Fix: pass `check_same_thread=False` to the per-request `sqlite3.connect()` (per-request connection in serialized SQLite mode is safe to disable the thread guard). Regression test reconstructs the cross-thread scenario directly without TestClient (which bridges every call through a single anyio portal pinned to one threadpool worker — masking the bug). Pre-fix the test fails with the production error string; post-fix it passes.
- **#485 Speculative ingest UX bundle.** Three small but compounding bugs made the speculative-ingest path feel broken on `:v0.20`:
  - `POST /speculative/approve/{id}` redirected to `/board/` (not a registered route — `/board/dashboard` is the canonical landing per `onboarding_gmail_config.py:72,121`); the approve work itself ran (synthetic jobs landed on the board) but the user-facing response was a FastAPI default `{"detail":"Not Found"}` JSON. Fixed to redirect to `/board/dashboard`. `regenerate` and `trash` redirects already targeted real routes (`/speculative/status/{id}` and `/ingest/`); no change there.
  - `/speculative/status/{id}` page promised auto-refresh every 5 seconds but stopped polling after the first tick. Root cause: `outerHTML` swap replaced the wrapper element carrying `id="status"` + `hx-trigger="every 5s"` with a fragment that didn't carry those attributes. Fixed by moving the trigger attrs onto each branch's outer element in `_status_fragment.html` so each render self-perpetuates; the `ready_for_review` branch's `window.location` redirect still fires.
  - Briefing was unreachable after leaving the review page. Fixed by making the materials route (`/materials/{fp}`) lifecycle-aware for synthetic rows: pre-prep, when no `prep_folder_path` exists but `speculative_briefing_folder` is set and the folder exists on disk, the materials view renders the spec folder's contents (`briefing.md` is classified as "Briefing (speculative)" by `_classify_file`). Post-prep, `prep_application.py` copies the spec folder's `briefing.md` into the prep folder during the synthetic-reuse path, so the materials view shows BOTH the raw deep-research brief and the prep-time merged briefing+fit_analysis as distinct artifacts. Synthetic rows on the dashboard now hyperlink the company name regardless of stage (gate uses the existing `[SPEC]` title-prefix convention already used for the SPEC badge — no new render-time coupling).

### Added
- **#487 `findajob.web.verify_auth` post-deploy auth-gate verifier + hard rule.** New Python module runnable as `docker exec <stack>-scheduler-1 python -m findajob.web.verify_auth`. Verifies (1) `FINDAJOB_AUTH_USER` / `FINDAJOB_AUTH_PASS` are non-empty in the runtime env, (2) an anonymous request to `/board/dashboard` returns `401` + `WWW-Authenticate: Basic`, (3) an authenticated request with the configured creds returns `200`. Distinct non-zero exit codes per failure mode (2/3/4/5) so downstream automation can react granularly. Codified as a hard rule in CLAUDE.md "Critical Architecture Rules" → "Auth Gate Must Be Verified Post-Deploy" and integrated into `docs/release-process.md` as the "Cohort deploy" section: every `docker compose up -d` is followed by the verifier; any non-zero exit triggers `docker compose down`. Triggered by an incident on 2026-05-07 where `findajob-test` was found internet-exposed without auth — no `FINDAJOB_AUTH_USER`/`PASS` in its `data/.env`, no `WWW-Authenticate` header in the public probe response.

### Changed
- **#462 `company_discoverer` cost-threshold ntfy now uses authoritative OpenRouter cost.** Pre-#471 (OpenRouter Native Migration Phase 2), the threshold-breach alert was sourced from a stderr-parsing function (`_extract_cost_usd`) that always returned `None` — the alert never fired. Phase 2 deleted the dead extractor and replaced it with `result.cost_usd` from `response.usage.cost`, making the alert functional, but no test or doc surface acknowledged the change. This release tightens `tests/discoverer/test_runner.py::test_run_emits_ntfy_when_threshold_breached` to assert the breach body contains both the run cost and the threshold value, adds a negative-path test (`cost ≤ threshold` does not fire the breach ntfy), and documents `DISCOVERY_COST_THRESHOLD_USD` in `data/.env.example`. No behavior change vs. v0.20.0 — verification + documentation only.

## [0.20.0] — 2026-05-07

Minor bump shipping the OpenRouter Native Migration epic (#469) close-out: the `blob42/aichat-ng` binary, its bundled config, and the cost-calibration stack are all gone. Every LLM call goes through `findajob.llm.openrouter.complete()`; every `cost_log.cost_usd` value is OpenRouter's `response.usage.cost` directly — no heuristic, no calibration multiplier, no `warming_up` state. The nav credits-remaining chip becomes a "$X.XX this month" spend chip; the dashboard burn-rate widget drops its runway-weeks projection. Production image is measurably smaller. **Migration-required** — see the Migration block below for the compose.yaml edit operators must apply on existing stacks. Operator's stack and `findajob-test` track `:latest`; tester stacks (alice, papa, dave, judy, tango) currently on `:v0.19` bump to `:v0.20` in this cohort wave.

### Refactor
- **#470 / Phase 1 of the OpenRouter Native Migration (#469):** added `src/findajob/llm/openrouter.py` — stdlib HTTP wrapper for OpenRouter chat completions. Public API: `complete()`, `CompletionResult`, typed `OpenRouterError`. Supports Anthropic `cache_control` on two axes (`cached_prefix` for shared content placed in the user message, `cache_system` for sufficiently large system prompts), provider pinning via `pin_provider`, retry-by-shape on 429/5xx/network (jittered exponential backoff, 3 attempts max), and direct `cost_log.cost_usd` writes from `response.usage.cost` via the new `cost_usd_override` keyword on `findajob.cost_tracking.log_call`. Ported `job_scorer` (highest call volume, simplest prompt) as proof-of-concept; the cached_prefix split (profile + feedback_block stable, JD/title/company per-call) sets the pattern for Phase 2's Opus-using ports where caching does cut cost (job_scorer's DeepSeek does not honor cache_control).
- **#471 OpenRouter Native Migration Phase 2** — All remaining LLM call sites (briefing_writer, resume_tailor, cover_letter_writer, recruiter_critic, fit_analyst, company_researcher, resume_change_reviewer, outreach_drafter, interview_prep, company_discoverer, candidate_led_briefing, speculative_roles_synth, voice_processor, onboarding interview) now route through `findajob.llm.openrouter.complete()`. Every `cost_log` row carries API-authoritative `usage.cost`. The 4 prep-stage Opus calls + outreach_drafter + interview_prep + speculative_roles_synth + onboarding interview pass `pin_provider="anthropic"` so same-role calls hit the prompt cache. Cross-role caching across the prep chain is deferred to #478 (the prep-chain restructuring is a separate epic). Closes #463 — onboarding interview turns now write `cost_log` rows via the canonical wrapper path (route handler reuses `add_turn_cost`'s connection to write the API-authoritative cost+tokens trio). Note: `speculative_roles_synth` uses `cached_prefix=profile+master_resume` (not `profile+briefing` as the plan first specified) — briefing differs per speculative request, so including it in the prefix would produce 0% cache hits.
- **#472 OpenRouter Native Migration Phase 3 — `aichat-ng` deleted, calibration stack retired (closes epic #469).** The `blob42/aichat-ng` binary, its bundled config (`ops/aichat-ng/`, `state/aichat_ng/` bind mount), the `AICHAT` entry in `findajob.paths`, the entrypoint config-seed + sed-substitution + scrub-embedding-client invocation, and `scripts/scrub_embedding_client.py` (dead post-#455) are all gone. Production image is measurably smaller. The cost-calibration stack — `cost_calibration` table, `scripts/poll_openrouter_credits.py`, the every-5-min `poll-openrouter-credits` cron, the `_multiplier()` / `current_calibration()` / `Calibration` / `runway_weeks()` helpers — was retired wholesale because OpenRouter's `response.usage.cost` (written natively by the wrapper since Phase 1) makes calibration obsolete. Three inline `cost_calibration` SELECTs at `web/routes/board.py:153`, `web/routes/board_actions.py:136`, `web/filters/registry.py:136` were rewritten to direct `SUM(cost_log.cost_usd)` in the same PR. The nav credits-remaining chip becomes a "spent this month" chip sourced from `cost_log` directly; the dashboard burn-rate widget loses its runway-weeks projection (kept "this week" + "projected this month"). All cost surfaces now read native API values — no heuristic, no multiplier, no `warming_up` state.

### Migration required
- **`docker compose pull && docker compose up -d` is the entire migration path for the schema + cron changes.** Existing stacks: `migrate_schema()` in `init_db.py` idempotently `DROP TABLE cost_calibration` on first boot post-upgrade; the every-5-min `poll-openrouter-credits` cron entry is removed from `crontab` automatically. Fresh installs never see the table.
- **Edit your stack's `compose.yaml` to drop the aichat-ng bind mount and the `HOME: /app` env, then recompose.** The deployed `compose.yaml` for an existing stack still carries `./state/aichat_ng:/app/.config/aichat_ng` under `volumes:` and `HOME: /app` under `environment:` — both were only there to position aichat-ng config. Sequence: (1) remove those two lines from `compose.yaml`, (2) `docker compose up -d` to recompose without the mount, (3) `rm -rf state/aichat_ng/` to reclaim disk. Skipping step 1 means Docker auto-recreates the empty source directory on the next `up -d`.
- **Cost numbers in the UI go from heuristic+multiplier to native API.** No more `warming_up` 7-day window — stacks have accurate cost from first prep run after upgrade. The nav chip text changes from "$X.XX credits" to "$X.XX this month"; the dashboard widget no longer shows runway weeks.

### Fixed
- **Opus 4.7 + Gemini 3 Flash rates corrected against empirical data (#460).** Post-#459 verification on the operator's stack (CoreWeave Technical Solutions Manager prep, 2026-05-05 21:45 UTC) measured `cost_log.cost_usd` 1.93× **over** authoritative — flipped from #458's 4.7× under. Root cause: #459 used Opus 4 pricing ($15/$75) for `openrouter:anthropic/claude-opus-4.7`, but Opus 4.7 launched at the lower $5/$25 tier (consistent across 5 Opus rows; ratio 0.333× rules out caching). Gemini 3 Flash Preview rate carried forward from the legacy Gemini 2 Flash entry ($0.10/$0.40), but Gemini 3 Flash actually prices ~5× higher ($0.55/$2.20 back-calculated from Vertex routing). Updated rates land both within ±5% of authoritative; total CoreWeave-style prep heuristic now ~$1.05 vs $1.11 dashboard.
- **Pricing table covers production OpenRouter model strings (#458).** Post-#48 verification (SK hynix America prep, 2026-05-05) revealed `cost_log.cost_usd` was 4.7× under authoritative — every opus / sonnet / gemini / perplexity call fell through to the default rate ($1/$5/Mtok) because `config/model_pricing.yaml` only had legacy `claude:` / `gemini:` / `perplexity:` entries from before the post-#250 OpenRouter cutover. Added `openrouter:`-prefixed entries for opus-4.7 ($15/$75), sonnet-4.6 ($3/$15), gemini-3-flash-preview ($0.10/$0.40), sonar-reasoning-pro ($2/$8), sonar-deep-research ($5/$20). Existing `openrouter:deepseek/deepseek-v3.2` ($0.27/$1.10) was already correct (only model with a working entry). Per-stage attribution was already correct pre-fix; only absolute amounts were biased. Perplexity per-request search fee (~$0.005/call) intentionally not modeled — keeps heuristic within ±30% target without a per-provider feature.

### Added
- **Unified LLM cost tracking across all aichat-ng call sites (#48).** Cost-log instrumentation now covers prep_application's 8 stages (company_researcher, briefing_writer, fit_analyst, resume_tailor, resume_change_reviewer, cover_letter_writer, recruiter_critic — including the briefing_writer retry path which writes 2 rows per the billing-truth rule), find_contacts (outreach_drafter), interview_prep, run_speculative_research (candidate_led_briefing + speculative_roles_synth), and company_discoverer. Pre-#48 only the scoring stage populated `cost_log.cost_usd` (~$0.0026/job × 13.5K rows); the higher-spend prep stages (~$2/job per body) had zero telemetry. Mechanism is the existing char-heuristic at `findajob.cost_tracking.log_call` — concurrency-safe by construction, ±20-30% absolute precision, reliable for relative comparisons (which prep stage costs most, week-over-week trend). Reuses `OPENROUTER_API_KEY`; no new credentials required. Unblocks #87 (real-time dashboard + ntfy projection) and #240 (cost-observability epic).
- **Centralized `role_model` helper at `findajob.cost_tracking.role_model`.** Hoisted from duplicated definitions in `scripts/triage.py:63` and `scripts/rescore_all.py:32`. Reads a role's frontmatter `model:` value with a `"unknown"` fallback for missing files or absent fields.

### Fixed
- **`scripts/rescore_all.py` populated cost_usd is no longer NULL (#48 AC 6).** The pre-#48 INSERT at line 271 left `cost_usd` NULL for all 3,384 rescore rows in production. Replaced with `log_call` so the char-heuristic populates the column going forward — non-zero on the LLM path, exactly 0.0 on the prefilter path (no LLM call to bill).

### Removed
- **Manual-ingest "Generate prep folder immediately" checkbox (#466).** The `/ingest/` form's auto-prep checkbox didn't reliably start prep on submission, and the workaround — clicking Flag-for-Prep on the dashboard like any other job — works fine. Removed `generate_folder` from `submit_manual` and `ingest_manual_job`, the `prep_launched` field on `IngestResult`, and the auto-prep dispatch + concurrency-deferred branch in `routes/ingest.py`. Manual-ingest rows always land at `stage='scored'`; operators flag for prep from the dashboard. Pure subtraction (~140 lines).

## [0.19.0] — 2026-05-05

Minor bump shipping the embedding/RAG retirement (#267 / #455) plus the operator-mode dashboard hardening for bind-mount edge cases (#359). User-visible: the project's only non-OpenRouter API-key dependency is gone — single-key onboarding (just OpenRouter) is now the entire required surface. The active scrub on existing stacks is fully idempotent and fail-open. Operator's stack and `findajob-test` track `:latest`; tester stacks (alice, papa, dave, judy, tango) currently on `:v0.18` bump to `:v0.19` in this cohort wave.

### Changed
- **Operator-mode dashboard hardened against bind-mount edge cases (#359).** `findajob.admin.jsonl_tail.tail_events` now catches `OSError` (covers `PermissionError`, not just `FileNotFoundError`) at both `os.path.getsize` and `open()`, so a chmod-stripped or mid-remount log file degrades to "no events" rather than 500-ing the page. `findajob.admin.stack_discovery.discover_stacks` catches `OSError` on `iterdir()` and returns `[]` with a logger warning rather than letting a restrictive `stacks_root` blank the dashboard. `findajob.admin.stack_health._parse_ts` coerces naïve ISO timestamps to UTC so a hand-edited or older log entry can't crash the render with a TypeError. The 24h-window event count now uses strict `>` (matching `_freshness`'s strict `<` — exactly-24h-ago is OUT of both windows) instead of mismatched `>=`. Operator-only impact; no schema or config changes.

### Removed
- **Embedding/RAG infrastructure retired entirely (#267 / #455).** Implements the decision recorded on #267: the `gemini-embed` aichat-ng client, the `rag_embedding_model` setting, the weekly `rag-rebuild` cron job, the `job_search_rag` index, and the `GOOGLE_API_KEY` collection step in onboarding are all gone. Closes the project's only non-OpenRouter API-key dependency, completing the milestone goal of single-key onboarding. Pipeline code never consumed embeddings (the index was REPL-only by design — see CLAUDE.md "RAG Policy"); operators who relied on `aichat-ng --rag job_search_rag` interactively can run a personal aichat-ng install outside the stack. Onboarding interview prompts no longer emit a Google API key, the `tester_google_key` column is dropped from `onboarding_sessions`, and the `gemini-embed` client + `rag_embedding_model` line are surgically removed from existing stacks' `config.yaml` on first boot post-upgrade. The first-seed plaintext-keys surface drops from 2 keys (OpenRouter + Google) to 1 (OpenRouter).

### Migration required
- **Active scrub of legacy embedding/RAG state on existing stacks (#455).** `docker compose pull && docker compose up -d` is the entire migration path. On first boot post-upgrade, `ops/entrypoint.sh` invokes `scripts/scrub_embedding_client.py` (fail-open) which removes the `gemini-embed` client block + `rag_embedding_model:` line from `state/aichat_ng/config.yaml` and deletes `state/aichat_ng/rags/job_search_rag.yaml`; the entrypoint also sed-deletes any `GOOGLE_API_KEY=` line from `state/data/.env`. The `onboarding_sessions.tester_google_key` column is dropped via `session_store.migrate_schema()` (idempotent `ALTER TABLE … DROP COLUMN` — SQLite 3.40.1 in the runtime image supports it directly). Idempotent: second-boot is a no-op. Operators with no `gemini-embed` usage notice nothing; operators who relied on `aichat-ng --rag job_search_rag` interactively will need to maintain their own untracked aichat-ng config outside the stack.

## [0.18.0] — 2026-05-05

Minor bump shipping per-tenant geography filtering for the three RapidAPI adapters (#372 / #450) plus two observability/correctness fixes: gmail per-sender logging + diagnostic override (#449) and the notify dead-feed detector false-positive correction. User-visible: each tenant can now write `config/target_locations.txt` to scope `jobs-api14`, `jobs-api14-indeed`, and `jsearch` queries to specific cities/regions instead of the hardcoded `United States`. Existing stacks without the file continue fetching `United States`-wide — no breaking change. Operator's stack and `findajob-test` track `:latest`; tester stacks (alice, papa, dave, judy, tango) currently on `:v0.17` bump to `:v0.18` in this cohort wave.

### Added
- **Per-tenant geography filter via `config/target_locations.txt` (#372 / #450).** One location per line; lines starting with `#` are comments. Missing/empty file falls back to `["United States"]` — no behavior change for stacks without the file. The onboarding interviewer Phase 3b now extracts machine-readable location values, and Phase 5 emits `target_locations.txt` whenever the operator selects RapidAPI as the active source. JSearch interprets `location=` as a metro area (e.g. NYC includes Brooklyn + NJ + CT commute zone — expected, not a bug); probe runs confirmed comma-joined and pipe-separated multi-location formats fail silently on both APIs, so per-location iteration is the only correct shape. `location=` is logged on every `jobsapi_fetched` / `jsearch_fetched` event for observability.
- `--gmail-since-days N` diagnostic flag on `scripts/triage.py` plus a `since_days` parameter on `fetch_gmail_jobs` / `fetch_new_messages` — triggers a SINCE-N-days IMAP search instead of the normal UID-incremental path. State still advances normally so the next scheduled run stays clean (#449).

### Changed
- **The three RapidAPI adapters (`jobs_api14`, `jobs_api14_indeed`, `jsearch`) now loop per-location × per-query**, calling the upstream API once for each combination instead of using the hardcoded `"United States"`. Per-call billing scales by `len(locations) × len(queries)`; an example 3 locations × 10 queries = 30 calls/day sits comfortably within RapidAPI PRO's 20K/month envelope (#450).
- **`gmail_messages_found` event now includes `by_sender` counts** so each of the configured Gmail senders is visible in `pipeline.jsonl`. A silent 0 from one sender is now distinguishable from a silent 0 across all senders (#449).

### Fixed
- **Notify dead-feed detector takes the max across all `jobs_fetched` events in the 25h window** rather than only `latest_fetch`. Eliminates the false-positive WARN that fired when a mid-day manual triage (gmail=0, healthy) followed a scheduled run that had already consumed the day's messages — a source is now only flagged dead if every run in the window returned 0 (commit `6f56807`).

### Migration required
- **`config/target_locations.txt` is opt-in (#450).** `docker compose pull && up -d` is the entire mandatory migration path; the fallback to `"United States"` preserves existing behavior. To opt into per-tenant geography, drop a file at `state/config/target_locations.txt` with one location per line. The file is read at each triage run; no container restart needed.

## [0.17.0] — 2026-05-04

Minor bump shipping the in-app notification dashboard + history (#440) plus the reject_reason vocabulary hygiene cleanup (#445). User-visible: notification bell + HTMX-polled unread badge in the top nav, new `/notifications/` page with kind/read filters, dashboard reads from a new `notifications` SQLite table; ntfy outages no longer lose the audit trail. Operator-required action: run the one-shot `reject_reason` cleanup script (idempotent) and add `"Company passed"` to operator stack's `config/reject_reasons.yaml`. Operator's stack and `findajob-test` track `:latest`; tester stacks (alice, papa, dave, judy, tango) currently on `:v0.15` bump straight to `:v0.17` in this cohort wave.

### Added
- **In-app notification dashboard + history (#440).** Pipeline notifications (daily stats, apply reminders, health checks, scoreboard, feedback reviews, CI alerts, discovery runs, gmail-auth failures, manual sends) now persist to a new `notifications` table. New `/notifications/` page renders a reverse-chronological list with filters by kind + read/unread state; bell icon + HTMX-polled unread badge in the top nav (every 60s); `POST /notifications/{id}/read` and `/notifications/mark-all-read` for triage. `scripts/notify.py:send()` now writes the row BEFORE the ntfy.sh POST so ntfy outages don't lose the audit trail (`delivery_status='failed'` + `delivery_error` populated when curl exits non-zero). Operator-mode `/admin/stacks/` table gains an "Unread notifs" column. Generalizes the ntfy fire-and-forget surface and lays the foundation for the rejection-detection signal coming in #362.
- `"Company passed"` added to `_DEFAULT_REJECT_REASONS` (#445). It was already the system-default fill-in at `findajob.web.routes.board_actions._board_not_selected` (when operator clicks "Not Selected" without picking a sub-reason) but wasn't in the canonical vocabulary, so it got flagged as a non-canonical drift value. Now first-class. Onboarding interviewer prompt updated to always emit it alongside the other operational universals (`Already Applied`, `Stale/Closed`, `Other`).

### Changed
- **`scripts/triage.py:437` writes `reject_reason='Other'` instead of `'Blank Company'` for unresolvable-company gmail_linkedin / jobsapi_indeed rows (#445).** Previously the triage path bypassed the `findajob.actions` write surface and inserted a non-canonical literal, polluting the user-facing reject_reason vocabulary with a pipeline-data-quality marker. Per-row diagnostic visibility is preserved via the existing `log_event("blank_company_rejected", source=...)` JSONL emission at the same call site.

### Removed
- Non-canonical `reject_reason` values from operator's stack DB (#445) — see Migration required.

### Migration required
- **New `notifications` table (#440).** `docker compose pull && docker compose up -d` is the entire migration path — `scripts/init_db.py` runs at container start and creates the table idempotently (`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS`). Existing notification call sites continue working unchanged; their rows start landing in the new table on the first cron firing post-restart. No backfill — historical notifications (pre-restart) are not reconstructable from `pipeline.jsonl` and stay absent from the dashboard.
- **One-shot `reject_reason` cleanup (#445).** After `docker compose pull && docker compose up -d` on each stack, run `docker compose exec -u 1000 scheduler python3 /app/scripts/cleanup_reject_reasons.py` once to normalize legacy non-canonical values. The script is idempotent (re-running is a no-op) and writes audit_log entries with `changed_by='reject_reason_cleanup_445'` so original values are recoverable. Dry-run available via `--dry-run`. Without the cleanup pass, the `/stats/feedback` page continues to show pre-existing non-canonical buckets ("Wrong Niche", "Blank Company", etc.) until they age out naturally — the cleanup is cosmetic-but-load-bearing for any analysis that joins on canonical reason vocabulary. Operator should also add `"Company passed"` to their stack's `config/reject_reasons.yaml` `reasons:` list (it's already in `_DEFAULT_REJECT_REASONS` for fresh installs without a yaml file). **Tester stacks** (alice, papa, dave, judy, tango) pinned at `:v0.15` won't see this until the next cohort wave; cleanup runs at bump time on each.

## [0.16.0] — 2026-05-04

Minor bump shipping the Google Sheets sync retirement (#331, closes #209) plus the aichat-ng config/catalog cleanup (#67). User-visible: the Sheet at the previously-synced ID stops updating — use the web UI at `/board/*` instead. Operator's stack and `findajob-test` track `:latest`; tester stacks (alice, papa, dave, judy, tango) currently on `:v0.15` stay on `:v0.15` until the next cohort wave.

### Changed
- **aichat-ng config slimmed to the two clients the pipeline actually uses (#67).** After the OpenRouter Phase 2 cutover (#250) the `openai`, `gemini` (chat), `groq`, and `xai` direct-client blocks in `ops/aichat-ng/config.yaml.example` were dead — every chat model now reaches its provider through `openrouter`. Removed those four blocks plus the corresponding env-var placeholders from `ops/entrypoint.sh`'s sed-seed loop (`OPENAI_API_KEY`, `GROQ_API_KEY`, `XAI_API_KEY` no longer substituted). Remaining direct clients are `openrouter` (every chat call) and `gemini-embed` (RAG embeddings only — REPL-opt-in; #267 tracks deprecation). First-seed now has 2 plaintext keys instead of 5. `data/.env.example` and the test fixtures dropped the dead env-var entries to match.
- **`ops/aichat-ng/models-override.yaml` trimmed from 25 providers to 1 (`openrouter`)** — 2080 lines → 468. The pipeline only ever resolves `model: openrouter:<provider>/<model>` strings; the other 24 provider sections (openai, claude, mistral, gemini chat, vertexai, bedrock, cohere, perplexity, etc.) were dead catalog data. Verified end-to-end against the installed `aichat-ng v0.31.0` binary: all 6 model strings invoked by `config/roles/*.md` resolve correctly post-trim. The lone exception (`openrouter:anthropic/claude-sonnet-4-6` referenced by `speculative_roles_synth.md` with a dash instead of dot) was a pre-existing typo unaffected by this change; filed for follow-up.

### Removed
- **Google Sheets sync path retired entirely (#331, closes #209).** The Sheet was the original read+write surface; #61 PR-B made it read-only and the web UI took over as the write surface; this change closes the loop by removing the read-only mirror. Deleted: `scripts/sync_sheet.py`, `scripts/setup_sheets.py`, the per-15-min `sync` cron entry (already absent from `ops/scheduled-jobs.yaml`), `tests/test_sync_sheet.py`, `tests/test_triage_sync_exit.py`, `docs/google-sheets.md`, the "Google Sheet Architecture" subsection in CLAUDE.md (board route table + stage descriptions kept under a renamed "Board Routes & Stage Lifecycle" section since they were canonical web-route info, not Sheet-specific), the "Google Sheet Layout" section in `docs/architecture.md`. Pruned: sync_sheet callers in `triage.py`, `prep_application.py`, `rescore_all.py`, `ingest_form.py`; `notify.py health-check`'s `sync_complete`/`sync_failed` checks; sheet env-var requirements + `sync_complete` assertion in `scripts/test_container_integration.sh`; setup steps from `docs/getting-started/{install-docker,install-native,prerequisites,state-migration,restore}.md`; `gsheets_creds.json` / `sheet_id.txt` from `.gitignore`, `data/.env.example`, `scripts/bootstrap.sh`. The `config/form_responses_sheet_id.txt` path is preserved — it gates `scripts/ingest_form.py` (Form-stragglers manual drain), which #62 retired but is kept callable.

### Migration required
- **`sync_sheet.py` and `setup_sheets.py` deleted (#331):** existing stacks need no action — the cron is gone (`docker compose pull && docker compose up -d` picks it up), and any orphaned `config/sheet_id.txt` / `config/gsheets_creds.json` files can be left in place or removed manually for cleanliness. The Google Sheet at the previously-synced ID is no longer updated; if you relied on it for phone-glance views, use `/board/*` in the web UI instead. Operators running the smoke check (`scripts/test_container_integration.sh`) no longer need the previously-required smoke-sheet ID / service-account env vars set; the script runs without them.

## [0.15.0] — 2026-05-03

Minor bump shipping the cohort wave: shared `RAPIDAPI_KEY` canonicalization, `JobsApi14IndeedAdapter` (Indeed restored via jobs-api14), per-adapter multi-page fetching (LinkedIn nextToken + JSearch num_pages), and the `JobsApi14IndeedAdapter` title-allowlist lift to config — plus #84 deterministic excluded-employer prefilter, #287 discoverer cost-guardrail recalibration, retirement of the derived `companies_of_interest.txt`, deletion of `env_migrate.py`, the local-dev `uv` standardization (#126), and a Docker-context refresh of `operations.md` / `architecture.md` / `scripts-reference.md`. Operator's stack and `findajob-test` track `:latest`; tester stacks (alice, papa, dave, judy, tango) currently on `:v0.13` bump straight to `:v0.15` in this cohort wave.

### Added
- `config/excluded_employers.yaml` — deterministic Stage 1 prefilter exclusion by company. Two-list shape: `exact:` (case-insensitive exact match) and `regex:` (compiled case-insensitive). Wires onboarding's "employers I'll never work for" signal from profile.md prose into the deterministic prefilter, consistent with the "Hard Rejects are Code" rule. Title hard-reject runs first so off-domain titles at excluded employers still report as title-rejects. Missing/empty file → no-op. Hits get `relevance_score=1`, no LLM call, `score_flag_reason="excluded_employer"` (#84)
- `JobsApi14IndeedAdapter` — Indeed coverage via jobs-api14 `/v2/indeed/search`. Restores pre-#408 Indeed pulls, tuned with `sortType=date` + adapter-side title-allowlist regex to compensate for the missing recency / experience-level / employment-type filters. 20 jobs/page (2× LinkedIn), inline JD ingestion. `source_label='jobsapi_indeed'` preserves DB row continuity. Active when `'jobs-api14-indeed'` is listed in `config/active_sources.txt` (#414)
- Shared `RAPIDAPI_KEY` env var as the canonical RapidAPI credential. Both `JobsApi14Adapter` and `JSearchAdapter` (and the new Indeed adapter) read it first, falling back to the legacy per-adapter vars (`JOBS_API14_KEY`, `JSEARCH_API_KEY`) if unset. Reflects the reality that RapidAPI uses one account-level key per user, not per-API (#414)
- `JOBS_API14_MAX_PAGES` env var — optional per-stack pagination ceiling for `JobsApi14Adapter` (LinkedIn endpoint). Default 1 (unchanged behavior). Loops over `meta.nextToken` up to N pages per query. Each additional page is one billed RapidAPI request (per-call billing — empirically confirmed on operator stack). PRO-tier operators (jobs-api14 PRO = 20k/mo) can safely set 3–5 for additive yield (2.25–3.75% of quota). Clamped to `[1, 20]`. `live_test()` stays single-page regardless of this setting (#414 PR2)
- `JSEARCH_NUM_PAGES` env var — optional per-stack pagination width for `JSearchAdapter`. Default 1 (unchanged behavior). Sets the `num_pages` API param so JSearch handles pagination server-side (single HTTP request per query, billed as N units). Empirically: N=3 returns ~27 jobs vs ~10 (~2.7x yield). PRO-tier operators (JSearch = 10k/mo) can safely set 3 (4.5% of quota). Clamped to `[1, 10]` (half of jobs-api14's ceiling because JSearch's PRO quota is half). `live_test()` stays at num_pages=1 regardless (#414 PR3)

### Changed
- Company-discoverer cost guardrail default lowered from `$10/run` → `$1/run` (`_DEFAULT_COST_THRESHOLD_USD` in `findajob.discoverer.runner`). PR-time smoke for #284 measured ~$0.10/run; the original $10 default carried ~50× more headroom than needed and would have suppressed real cost-anomaly signal. Operators with `DISCOVERY_COST_THRESHOLD_USD` set in `data/.env` are unaffected. Annual envelope revised from ~$260/year/stack to ~$5/year/stack (52 runs × ~$0.10) (#287)
- `JobsApi14IndeedAdapter` title allowlist lifted from a hardcoded engineering-tuned regex (`_TITLE_ALLOW_PATTERN`) to the optional `indeed_title_allow:` key in `config/prefilter_rules.yaml`. Missing/empty key = no post-filter (allow-all). Field-specific example blocks for engineering, healthcare, social-work, and education candidates included in `prefilter_rules.yaml.example`. Restores domain-neutrality of the pipeline per CLAUDE.md "PII / Domain-Neutrality — HARD RULES" (#417)
- Local-dev tooling standardized on `uv` — `uv sync` for dev deps, `uv run` for pytest / ruff / mypy / uvicorn. Docker image still uses `pip install -e .` inside the container (no change to release pipeline). Contributor docs and `pyproject.toml` updated; existing virtualenv-based dev loops continue to work, but the documented path is `uv sync` (#126)
- `docs/operations.md`, `docs/architecture.md`, and `docs/scripts-reference.md` refreshed for Docker-canonical run mode. `operations.md` gains parallel `## Docker Operations (Compose)` and `## Native Operations (systemd)` sections; commands shown in `docker compose exec scheduler …` form; `architecture.md` adds a `## Scheduler` subsection naming `ops/scheduled-jobs.yaml` as canonical schedule source; `scripts-reference.md` gains a `Manual run:` line per script. Native install stays supported as fallback (#76)
- `docs/usage/expanding-sources.md` — new dedicated guide for adding LinkedIn saved-search alerts to multiply `gmail_linkedin` ingestion volume. Cross-field example bundle (engineering / healthcare / social work / education / skilled trades). Cross-linked from `docs/usage.md` and registered in the `/docs/` web viewer (#275)

### Removed
- `findajob.onboarding.env_migrate.migrate_rapidapi_key_env()` and its startup invocation in `findajob.web.app`. The v0.14 helper renamed `RAPIDAPI_KEY` → `JOBS_API14_KEY` on every container boot, which became the inverse of #414's canonical-name direction. Adapter + legacy-fetcher fallback (introduced alongside #414) covers the same compatibility surface without rewriting `data/.env` (#416)
- `config/companies_of_interest.txt` — the derived file is no longer written by the onboarding injector or read by `findajob.config_loader`. `load_companies_of_interest()` now parses Tier 1 directly from `config/target_companies.md` at runtime (single source of truth). Removed: `config/companies_of_interest.txt.example`, `scripts/seed_companies_of_interest.py`, `findajob.onboarding.injector.derive_companies_of_interest` and its `_COMPANIES_OF_INTEREST_DEST` constant. Tier 1 parser logic moved to `findajob.config_loader.parse_target_companies_tier1()` with full test coverage (#211)

### Migration required
- **Existing stacks pulling next minor:** legacy `JOBS_API14_KEY` / `JSEARCH_API_KEY` continue to work — no action required to keep current adapter configs running. To start using `RAPIDAPI_KEY` as the canonical name, copy the existing legacy var's value to `RAPIDAPI_KEY=` in `data/.env` (operators can also remove the legacy vars once migrated, but they're harmless if left).
- **Stacks where v0.14's auto-rename already fired** (have `JOBS_API14_KEY` set, `RAPIDAPI_KEY` absent): no action required. The legacy var continues to be read via fallback. Adopt the canonical name on your next manual edit if you want one.
- **To enable the new Indeed adapter:** add `jobs-api14-indeed` as a new line in `config/active_sources.txt` and restart the stack. No new credentials needed (shares jobs-api14's account).
- **To opt into multi-page LinkedIn fetching:** add `JOBS_API14_MAX_PAGES=3` (or up to 5) to `data/.env` and restart the stack. PRO-tier operators only; BASIC stays at default 1 to avoid quota burn. No action required for default behavior.
- **To opt into JSearch multi-page fetching:** add `JSEARCH_NUM_PAGES=3` to `data/.env` and restart the stack. PRO-tier operators only; BASIC stays at default 1 to avoid quota burn. No action required for default behavior.
- **`JobsApi14IndeedAdapter` allowlist lift (#417):** if your stack runs the Indeed adapter (`jobs-api14-indeed` in `config/active_sources.txt`), the engineering-tuned hardcoded title allowlist is gone. Without configuration, the adapter now allows ALL Indeed titles through (89% noise for engineering candidates per pre-#414 measurement). To preserve operator's pre-#417 behavior, add the engineering-default `indeed_title_allow:` block from `config/prefilter_rules.yaml.example` to your `config/prefilter_rules.yaml`. For non-engineering candidates, replace the engineering block with the field-specific example provided. Stacks not running the Indeed adapter are unaffected.
- **`companies_of_interest.txt` retired (#211):** the derived file is no longer read by the pipeline. `notify.py` mis-score health check + `sync_sheet.py` archival exception now read Tier 1 directly from `config/target_companies.md`. **Existing stacks need no action** — the orphaned `config/companies_of_interest.txt` file can be left in place (ignored) or deleted manually for cleanliness. Per-stack `target_companies.md` already exists from prior onboarding; if you've manually edited `companies_of_interest.txt` since onboarding (rare), reconcile those edits into `target_companies.md` Tier 1 to preserve them.
